Current Affairs Commentary

The Last Chance for Opium Addicts to Extricate Themselves 11

— Du

Since the central government resolved to abolish the Anti-Opium Committee and have Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Military Council concurrently serve as the Director-General of Anti-Opium, using military law to promote the anti-opium policy, its determination to deeply hate and eradicate it has already been seen by all. Chiang is issuing educational orders and enforcing laws step by step. With the trend of the times, the effects are gradually becoming visible. In terms of planting, the inland provinces are of course absolutely prohibited, and remote areas are also subject to scheduled prohibitions. In terms of transportation and sales, the current output is under unified control, and the passing on of secrets is strictly prohibited. For addicts, the goal is to gradually eliminate addiction, with the issuance of licenses for limited consumption until 1940, when planting, transporting, selling, and smoking will all be completely eliminated without pardon. This is a reasonable and well-considered approach, not a hasty undertaking. The repeated orders in official documents and the detailed and comprehensive exhortations show the authorities' dedication to avoid embarrassing people. We in the news industry believe that this is the only good policy and are happy to promote it with words and convey its implications. We dare not tire of repeating it.

Ordinary people do not know the harm of opium, and those who know it still fail to restrain themselves and lightly engage in it do so because the habit has been around for a long time, the temptation is strong, and addiction is easy. This is true for those who are old and sick. Young men and women who linger in pavilions after dancing and singing often quench their thirst with poison and throw themselves into the net when they think of finding excitement. At first, they laugh at the attempt, but in the end, they fall into the black book and find it difficult to return. Is this not even more disastrous? Since ancient times, those who have talked about banning opium have always thought of starting with the source. However, unscrupulous merchants either take advantage of operations as a shortcut to starting a business or rely on selling and smoking as a means of making a living. They do not hesitate to break the law and try to obstruct in every possible way. It is difficult to expect the eradication of the pervasive poisonous atmosphere unless a unanimous determination is made to strike hard. Now, the authorities are banning planting and blocking sources, registering and controlling sales and smoking, confiscating property to scare away their profit-making ideas, and sentencing to death to ensure the ultimate sanction. If all levels of the government are committed to their duties and move quickly, it may not be difficult for the brokers to wash their hands and the wicked to restrain themselves. As for the addicts, under such strict scrutiny, those who are tempted can avoid addiction, and those who are not deeply addicted can be cured immediately. However, for those who are old, sick, and accumulate gradually, it is difficult to get rid of in a hurry. The authorities have implemented a gradual cessation method by issuing licenses, which is a proper way to seek relief for these people. Even during the reporting period, they are still allowed to register retroactively, which can be said to be a careful consideration. If they still hold the intention of waiting and seeing and trying to be lucky, not only will they fail to live up to the country, but will they not love themselves? Time and situation are pressing. The opportunity is fleeting. Quickly rise up and seek the last chance, and there is no room for hesitation.

Remnant Bandits in Western Shanxi Attempt to Cross the River to Shaanxi and Are Repelled; Various Armies Pursue and Suppress Lin Biao's Bandits in Pu County; Xu and Liu's Remnants Reassemble in Shuangchi Town 12

(Taiyuan) About 2,000 bandits have gathered again in places such as Damaijiao and Shuangchi Town. It seems that the remnants of Xu and Liu who fled south from Zhongyang have joined forces with the remnants of Zhongyang and the bandits in the county of Shilou. Yan ordered the various armies to quickly construct blockhouses around the bandit strongholds to prepare for blockade and suppression and to avoid proliferation. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 19th)

(Xi'an) According to military news from Hancheng, more than 1,000 remnant bandits from Shanxi attempted to cross the Yellow River from the Yumengkou area on the 12th of this month. The troops under Sun, the commander of our army stationed in Hancheng, launched a fierce attack on the bandits while they were crossing the river. Most of the bandits were killed, and the remnant bandits were all wounded and returned to cross the river. They did not dare to look at the west bank again. Japanese Foreign Minister Arita Decides on Diplomatic Policy, Focusing on China and Russia, Using Economic and Cultural Means 14

(Nanjing) Foreign Minister Arita, after clarifying his diplomatic policy at the 68th Diet, convened a meeting of senior Foreign Ministry officials on the 18th at his official residence for careful discussions. It was decided that another meeting would be held on the 21st to finalize the decision. The spirit of his speech follows the Emperor's Rescript, based on a world peace policy. His specific adjustments adopt an independent and proactive approach, focusing on policies toward China and the Soviet Union. Regarding China, it is based on the Three Principles, aiming to adjust national relations. Regarding Soviet relations, it follows the traditional policy, striving to advocate for the withdrawal of Soviet forces from the Far East. China, Japan, and Manchukuo should cooperate based on common principles, absolutely excluding communist ideology from East Asia. The main points of his speech are as follows:

(A) Diplomatic Foundation: Promoting the survival and development of the Japanese nation, while striving to foster peaceful and friendly relations with other powers.

(1) Policy Towards the Soviet Union: Recently, the Soviet government has adopted an active stance towards East Asia, especially "Manchukuo." This requires attention to maintain stability in East Asia. The Japanese government believes that the Red Army does not need to be stationed in the Far East, so it should withdraw. Withdrawing unnecessary Red Army forces would eliminate the root causes of unfortunate incidents on the Soviet-Manchukuo border. The Japanese government can also promptly resolve various pending issues between Japan and the Soviet Union to establish friendly relations between the two countries, which is what we earnestly hope for.

(2) Policy Towards China: The rapid establishment of normal relations between Japan, China, and Manchukuo is what we have always hoped for. However, rampant communism now directly threatens North China and "Manchukuo." The Japanese government cannot but have significant concerns for the stability of East Asia.

(3) Relations with Britain and the United States: Japan and the United States are two major friendly nations separated by the ocean, and there are no problems that cannot be resolved through diplomatic means. Anglo-Japanese relations are extremely complex in terms of trade. Therefore, the British and Japanese governments are frankly exchanging views on adjusting relationships such as insufficient markets and resources. Our reasonable demands will certainly be realized.

(B) Trade Relations: Currently, market closures and collusion of economic alliances in the world hinder Japan's trade development and are extremely harmful. The Japanese government should demand the opening of markets to the world, abolish exclusionary alliances, and strive to implement the principles of free trade.

(C) Cultural Work: To live in harmony with other countries and make the world understand the Japanese national character, cultural work is considered a side aspect of diplomacy, which is necessary. Since Japan is an existing force for stability in East Asia, its cultural essence should be recognized by the world, which is an urgent task. (Kyodo News Agency, 19th)

(Tokyo) The 69th Diet, convened on May 1st, will hold its opening ceremony on May 4th and its closing ceremony on May 25th. Prime Minister Hirota's policy speech and Foreign Minister Arita's foreign policy speech will be delivered at 10:00 AM in the House of Peers and at 1:00 PM in the House of Representatives. However, Finance Minister Baba's financial speech will only be delivered in the House of Representatives. (Dentsu News Agency, 9th)

Decline of Chinese Tea in Java Due to Dumping of Local Tea and Taiwanese Tea 32

(Nanjing) The sales of Chinese tea in Java used to be in the leading position. However, in recent years, due to competition from Dutch East Indies local tea and the dumping of Taiwanese tea, the impact has been very significant. According to the latest survey, the current market price of Taiwanese tea in Java is 20 Japanese yen per picul, while the price of Chinese tea is 40 yuan. Although the general literati love Chinese tea, they ultimately have to choose the former due to its high price. The import volume of Chinese tea in the same period last year was 803,000 kg, while Taiwanese tea reached 1,449,011 kg. Therefore, Chinese tea has been overwhelmed. As a result, many overseas Chinese tea shops have closed down, and over ten thousand overseas Chinese who depend on the tea market for a living have become unemployed and returned to their country. If this continues, Chinese tea is likely to disappear from the Dutch East Indies market in one or two years. It is said that our government authorities are now trying to find ways to help. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 19th)

British Prime Minister Baldwin Proposes Military Sanctions Against Aggressor Nations; Collective Security System Will Never Succeed Unless All Countries Are Willing to Sacrifice 34

(London) Prime Minister Baldwin said in a speech in Worcester yesterday that the collective security system will never succeed unless the participating countries are prepared to simultaneously impose military sanctions on aggressors, even if it means war. He also reiterated Britain's position on the Italo-Ethiopian war, emphasizing that Britain urgently needs to expand its military. He also strongly condemned the Italian army's use of poison gas in East Africa.

Italian Army's Use of Poison Gas Greatly Endangers Civilization; Europe Now at a Critical Juncture 35

The Prime Minister said that if Europe sees war again and uses poison gas, the destruction of its civilization is even more certain. He believes that when this new war ends, the people of all countries, driven by public anger and the suffering of war, will rise up to destroy the governments of Europe, and we will encounter a state of chaos and resistance against the evil deeds of those in high positions.

The Prime Minister said that when he should retire, he will retire. He also said that he can count on one hand the number of people outside the madhouse who are willing to take his place. The audience cheered loudly. The Prime Minister mentioned the current international situation, saying that the two most important things in the recent weeks are (1) Germany's rearmament and (2) the mockery of the League of Nations, which have proven that the expansion of Britain's military is absolutely necessary. If Britain still wants to fulfill its obligations to the League of Nations and maintain its position in the world, it must take this step. In the recent general election, the government was entrusted by the people to carry out the task of rearmament.

At the end of the European War, it was easy to implement sanctions and make the aggressor immediately succumb to world pressure. But today's League of Nations is no longer comparable to the League of Nations when it was first created. At least three major countries, namely the United States, Germany, and Japan, do not participate in the League of Nations. The non-participation of these three major countries reduces the strength of the implementation of sanctions. The League of Nations could not prevent the Italo-Ethiopian War, but took joint action to declare Italy an aggressor and imposed certain sanctions. However, if one of the two belligerents is determined to wage war without submitting the case's differences for discussion or accepting arbitration, it seems that there is no powerful mechanism to end this war. Furthermore, the implementation of sanctions is slow, and if the final sanction, namely blockade or force, cannot be used as an aid, the sanctions currently implemented have greatly lost their power. But today, it is difficult to say how the blockade can obtain the consent of all the countries that organized the League of Nations.

Italians now have a tendency to attribute praise and blame to individuals for the actions of the League of Nations, but they do not know that the League of Nations' actions are the result of collective efforts. He once read an Italian newspaper that criticized British Foreign Secretary Eden for being engaged in anti-Italian policies, which showed that he did not understand right and wrong and made people sigh. This attack contains two misunderstandings that he would like to dispel: (1) The foreign policy conducted by the Foreign Secretary is not his personal policy, but the policy determined by the entire British government and supported by the majority of the British people. (2) This is not an anti-Italian policy, and its goal is not to make Italy fail or succumb, but to uphold the League of Nations. We want the League of Nations to become the law of the world. This is our goal. Therefore, when the League of Nations is in danger of being destroyed, we are responsible for doing our best to help the League of Nations. This is our only desire for this matter. He believes that the rest of the world will fully understand this. If Italians think that our policy aims to make them fail or succumb, then they are greatly mistaken.

The Prime Minister concluded by mentioning the collective security system, saying that we are currently working hard to operate it and will continue to operate it. We have not yet reached our goal, and we must continue to move forward to achieve it. The collective security system will never succeed unless the participating countries are prepared to simultaneously impose military sanctions on aggressors, even if it means war. This means that the countries participating in the collective security system must be prepared at any time.

The two belligerent countries accuse each other of violating the war regulations. The League of Nations will now conduct a fair investigation. If the claim that poison gas was used is confirmed, and we now have various reasons to believe it is confirmed, then it endangers the world and is no small matter. If a major European country ignores its signature on the public opposition to the use of this poison gas and uses it in Africa, then how can we be sure that it will not be used in Europe in the future? European cities are more densely populated than Abyssinia, and the harm they suffer will be far greater. If Europe sees war again and uses poison gas to fight, the destruction of its civilization is even more certain. He believes that if this is used, then when the war ends, the people of all countries, driven by public anger and the suffering of war, will rise up to destroy the governments of Europe, and we will encounter a state of chaos and resistance against the evil deeds of those in high positions.

European leaders must realize what the League of Nations is lacking in their efforts to maintain peace, how it can be strengthened, how the collective security system can be implemented, and what kind of guarantees can be obtained to prevent poison gas from being used in Europe. But what opportunities do we have now? He does not want to say that the omens are completely unfavorable. There is now dense haze in many places in the sky. However, we have received proposals from the French and German governments and are now paying the most serious attention to them. The same proposal comes from two major European countries at the same time, which is indeed innovative. Who is better than Britain to investigate this issue and seek to bring the two countries closer together? When he was in office, he often talked about the difficulties of dictatorships, because he believed that the dictatorship system would eventually cause more harm than it eliminated. The German dictator Hitler, today, his position holds the power to clear the haze of all of Europe, which is actually greater than anyone in Europe. Mr. Xi's power can actually do this. God allows Mr. Xi to do it. If Mr. Xi is willing to do it, then there will be no trace of what Britain can do left behind. He believes that Mr. Xi has this ambition, and no one in Europe does not want to cooperate with him, because the people of Europe now all yearn for peace and are all terrified of the suffering of war.

The Prime Minister concluded by saying that the next few months are a critical period for life and death. (Reuters, 19th)

Italian Peace Terms Released by League of Nations 36

(Geneva) Italy submitted its preliminary terms for peace to the Committee of Thirteen on the 16th of this month. The content included a total of four items, which were recently released by the Secretariat of the League of Nations.

Italy agrees to immediately begin ceasefire negotiations, or the military authorities of both sides will negotiate a ceasefire agreement, or the representatives of the two countries will negotiate preliminary peace terms, all of which are possible. However, the negotiation time required for a ceasefire agreement must be very long, just like the negotiation of peace terms. At the same time, special measures must be negotiated to ensure the safety of the Italian army. Italy therefore advocates that it is more appropriate to negotiate preliminary peace terms immediately.

During the negotiations, the Italian delegation believes that the war situation since the outbreak of the war six months ago must be taken into account, and the Committee of Thirteen cannot ignore this level.

The Italian delegation believes that the only appropriate method is for the two parties involved, Italy and Ethiopia, to conduct direct negotiations. The location should be in Ouchy, near Lausanne, Switzerland. Italy also considers all measures to notify the Committee of Thirteen of the progress of the negotiations at any time.

The Italian delegation expressed the hope that the results of these negotiations will enable Italy to actively cooperate with the League of Nations in the general situation. (Havas, 18th)

(Geneva) The Thirteen-Nation Committee today passed a report on the failure of mediation in the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, without assigning blame for the failure. Prior to the vote, Committee Chairman Madariaga consulted with representatives from both Italy and Ethiopia on the report's content. The report will be submitted to the League of Nations Council for discussion on Monday afternoon. At the request of British Foreign Secretary Eden, the League of Nations' committee of experts will also meet on Monday morning to study the effectiveness of sanctions against Italy and submit a report to the Council, to be considered together with the Thirteen-Nation Committee's report. (National Telegram, 18th)

(Geneva) The Thirteen-Nation Committee met this afternoon and unanimously passed the report drafted by Chairman Madariaga, which will be submitted to the League of Nations Council for discussion next Monday. The report documents the failure of the committee to mediate the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. All documents related to Madariaga's negotiations with representatives from Italy and Ethiopia have been included, and the report mentions Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's invitation for Madariaga to meet with him in Rome. The report also addresses the issue of the Italian army's use of poisonous gas and the violation of wartime laws by both Italian and Ethiopian forces. Regarding this issue, the chairman of the Thirteen-Nation Committee, Madariaga, condemned Mr. Huber, president of the International Red Cross, because the Thirteen-Nation Committee had previously requested him to provide documents regarding the brutal acts of both Italian and Ethiopian forces, but was refused, preventing the Thirteen-Nation Committee from conducting an investigation. As for the Ethiopian government's citation of the testimony of Polish doctor Boro to prove the brutal acts of the Italian army, the Thirteen-Nation Committee's Polish representative, Komarnicki, provided unfavorable information about Boro's integrity. The committee considered Boro's statements unreliable and therefore did not include them in the report. (Havas, 18th)

(Geneva) The Thirteen-Nation Committee today passed the report submitted by the League of Nations experts regarding the use of poisonous gas in East Africa. It contains the Ethiopian accusations against the Italian army and the report submitted to the League of Nations by the United Kingdom. The committee also passed the report by Chairman Madariaga and League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol declaring the failure of mediation in the East African war. Today's meeting was brief and largely a formality, lacking the tension of previous sessions. Madariaga simply announced that the Ethiopian representative was eager for Italy to declare its terms for reconciliation, but after an hour of talks between the two countries' representatives, it was clear that negotiations could not proceed in the spirit of the League of Nations. Italian Chief Delegate Aloisi then responded, saying that Italy deeply hoped to cooperate with other countries in the League of Nations once the war with Ethiopia ended. (Reuters, 18th)

(Geneva) The Thirteen-Nation Committee of the League of Nations Council requested Italy and Ethiopia on the 10th of this month not to adopt any methods of warfare that violate international agreements. The governments of both countries have submitted replies. Committee Chairman Madariaga has also sent a letter to the Italian government, requesting a detailed explanation of the country's army's use of poisonous gas. It stated, "While your country's reply provided a detailed response regarding the bombing of rescue teams, it made no mention of the use of gas. Although the final paragraph states, 'If the enemy disregards law and morality and resorts to brutal acts, the Italian army will have no choice but to punish them,' this cannot be used as an excuse to use suffocating gas, poisonous gas, and similar gases." In addition, the Italian government, because its Colonel Liberati had previously suffered injuries from Dum Dum bullets, lodged a protest with League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol. (Havas, 19th)

(Geneva) Chairman Madariaga of the Thirteen-Nation Committee of the League of Nations Council, after reviewing the committee's decision, sent a letter to Mr. Huber, president of the International Red Cross, expressing regret for the organization's refusal to provide relevant documents regarding the methods of warfare used by the Italian and Ethiopian forces. He stated that the organization's reason for refusing, namely maintaining neutrality, was understandable. However, he continued, "It is surprising that the Thirteen-Nation Committee, acting in the name of the League of Nations Council, was met with this kind of excuse." (Havas, 19th)

(Geneva) French Minister without Portfolio, Peng Gu, held talks today with Italian representative Aloisi, Soviet representative (and Soviet Ambassador to France) Potemkin, Romanian representative Antoniade, and Polish representative Komarnicki. The discussion centered on the situation at the League of Nations Council meeting next Monday. It is expected that the Council will make two decisions on that day. In the morning, the Chairman of the Thirteen-Nation Committee, Madariaga, will present his report, and representatives from Italy and Ethiopia will deliver speeches. In the afternoon, after other countries' representatives express their opinions, a resolution will be passed to conclude the discussion. Alternatively, it is possible that the Chairman of the Council, Australian representative Bruce, will deliver a speech instead of a resolution. (Havas, 18th)

Addis Ababa - It is reported today that Italian forces in the south have now occupied Qiqiqa, northeast of Harar. The Ethiopian government, fearing that the capital may be attacked, is currently seriously considering moving the capital to the west. (Reuters, 19th)

(Rome) According to semi-official sources, Italian forces have occupied Harar. Addis Ababa - Ethiopia is determined to fight to the end in its resistance against Italy. Today, Addis Ababa is still frantically conscripting disorganized troops in the streets, sending them north to try to stop the advance of the Italian forces. Mayor Tigara is also personally giving moving speeches in the streets, calling on the people to enlist. The hopelessness of the war is completely evident. The Belgian technical advisors in the Ethiopian army have already begun their return journey, boarding a train today to Djibouti. (National Telegram, 18th)

Addis Ababa - The official announcement acknowledges foreign reports that there are internal disagreements within the government and states that the government continues to communicate and exchange opinions with the Ethiopian Emperor. The announcement also confirms reports that the Emperor intends to move the capital to the west, but the name of the city cannot be announced. It is widely believed that this decision demonstrates the Emperor's insistence on resisting to the end, even if the capital is unfortunately lost, this determination will not waver. (National Telegram, 18th)

Inter-American Peace Conference: Argentine Foreign Minister Proposes Draft Treaty 42

Buenos Aires - The Inter-American Peace Conference is about to be convened. Foreign Minister Lamas has submitted a draft treaty to the conference's preparatory committee to consolidate peace. The main points are as follows: 1. Consolidate and expand the arbitration system; 2. Oppose "armed peace"; 3. Abolish violence; 4. Implement sanctions against aggressor countries, but without endangering the neutrality of the treaty countries; 5. The Kellogg-Briand Pact, the League of Nations Covenant, and this draft treaty should be linked together; 6. Abolish tariff wars; 7. The restrictions imposed by various countries on the shipping industry should be reduced to facilitate the flow of goods. Regarding the consolidation and expansion of the arbitration system, Lamas argues that this system should apply equally to legal and non-legal issues, without distinction. In addition, he also argues that all countries in the Americas, as well as other countries in the world, should be able to join this treaty. (Havas, 18th)

Political Turmoil Brewing in Poland: Military and Civilian Factions in Conflict 47

Warsaw - After the clash between unemployed people and police in Lviv on the 14th of this month, the "Colonel's faction" and the civilian cabinet members are increasingly in conflict. There may be a cabinet reshuffle, in which the position of Interior Minister Raczkiewicz is particularly unstable. However, even if a cabinet crisis occurs, it is possible that the Inspector General of the Army Education Department, Zymierski, and the Army Chief of Staff, Sosnkowski, will step forward to mediate, because they did not sign the resolution passed by the Veterans' Association, which called for the formation of a political party to implement the ideals of the late Marshal Piłsudski. The civil faction and the "Colonel's faction" have been at odds since the death of Marshal Piłsudski. The "Colonel's faction" originally advocated abolishing the party system and organizing a parliament of professional groups based on local interests to replace the National Assembly. The moderates, i.e., the civil faction, such as Prime Minister Gościński and Deputy Prime Minister and Finance Minister Kwiatkowski, wanted the cabinet to cooperate with the left wing to deal with the situation. The "Colonel's faction" opposed this policy, and since the Lviv incident, their opposition has become more intense. In addition, the semi-official Polish Daily (the mouthpiece of the "Colonel's faction") has also accused the current cabinet of being weak and incompetent and said that it should retreat from the scene. They have even attacked President Mościcki. Prime Minister Gościński then banned the publication of the newspaper, making the confrontation between the two sides even more obvious. Political figures say that Interior Minister Raczkiewicz should be responsible for the Lviv incident and should resign before Labor Day on May 1st, making a cabinet reshuffle inevitable. (Havas, 19th)

Warsaw - Prime Minister Gościński, who was originally scheduled to go to the Hungarian capital this morning at 8:00 AM on a return visit, unexpectedly postponed his departure due to "physical discomfort." It is generally believed that this move was caused by the semi-official Polish Daily's fierce criticism of Gościński after the clash between unemployed people and police in Lviv on April 14th, which has even led to the possibility of a cabinet crisis. The Prime Minister therefore postponed his departure. The cause of the April 14th Lviv conflict is as follows: On that day, a group of unemployed people held a demonstration and threw bricks at major buildings. A conflict occurred with the police, who opened fire, killing two workers belonging to the "Labor Front" (one of whom was Korczak) and injuring many others. When the deceased Korczak was buried on April 16th, the demonstrating crowd clashed with the police again. The Polish Daily then began to criticize the cabinet, accusing it of improper measures. The press censor also ordered the newspaper to be suspended this morning. It is reported that the cabinet has had partial changes due to the impact of the Lviv incident, i.e., the struggle between the cabinet and the "Colonel's faction" has begun. (The "Colonel's faction" refers to the old subordinates of the late military minister, the former Polish dictator Marshal Piłsudski, most of whom are colonels, hence the name.) The Polish Daily is one of the main mouthpieces of the "Colonel's faction." (Havas, 19th)

Miscellaneous Notes on Rural Hubei 64

(Special Correspondent for This Newspaper: Cheng Jun)

Yangxin After the Calamity

Yangxin suffered the most during the bandit disasters in Hubei Province in the past, and the destruction of the rural areas was the most severe. I, the reporter, personally visited the area, eager to interview the victims and understand their suffering. However, I was hindered by heavy rain and spent two gloomy days in the city. This morning (the 2nd), after the rain cleared and the sky brightened, I left the West Gate, passed through Songshunao, Guanqiao, Ditianpu, and finally reached Zhanbutou, walking twenty-nine li. Along the way, the number of碉堡 (fortified houses) outnumbered civilian houses, and the severity of the disaster could be imagined. Zhanbutou is a small market town with about sixty or seventy households. It uses tens of thousands of pine trees as fences to defend against bandits. It can be described as the most novel defensive work besides 碉堡. There are few pedestrians on the road, and it is impossible to find food in the town. I offered two 角 (jiao, unit of currency) as payment to buy wheat cakes, but they had no change. Women in tattered clothes digging grass by the roadside were everywhere. When asked, they said they were going to use it to fill their stomachs. This grass is commonly known as red flower grass and is used to feed pigs. Now, they are using it to fill their bellies. It was heartbreaking to hear, but they didn't seem to mind much. According to them, there was a great disaster the year before, and the people had exhausted all means of survival. Although the government provided relief, many still starved to death. In Mushigang and Paishi alone, more than 3,000 people starved to death. More than 1,000 people died of starvation after being taken to the urban area, and more than 1,000 people died of starvation in Sanxikou, mostly the elderly, weak, women, and children. "We are fortunate to be able to dig grass to eat," they said. I also met an old man resting by the side of the road and chatted with him. According to him, there have recently been animal disasters in the mountainous areas. Because there are no people in the areas near the mountains, wild animals have been able to breed. The most common are wild boars and muntjacs, which come out of the mountains in groups of dozens at night to forage for food. As a result, the sweet potatoes and wheat in the nearby farmland are completely unharvested. The government prohibits the use of guns, and hunters have no way to hunt them. By the time I returned to the city, it was already noon. I went to visit the group farm. The farm is fifteen li away from the city, and there are no civilian houses along the way. Occasionally, there are one or two dilapidated walls standing among the desolate smoke and weeds. When I asked a passerby, he said that in the past, the people between the county seat and Mushigang, a distance of thirty li, were prosperous, and the houses were lined up one after another. Now, they have all been burned down. The market town of Mushigang, with more than 200 households, has also been reduced to ashes, with only the ashes of the fire remaining to commemorate it. There were fewer pedestrians on the road than in the western countryside. They were all selling firewood, and most of them were women and children. An old woman of sixty was hunched over carrying firewood, walking and resting. She said that both of her sons had been killed, and her daughter-in-law had been sold. Now, she is all alone and can only eke out a living by selling firewood. When asked about the price of the firewood, it was only one 角. It was so sad! It is said that the red bandits in the county have been wiped out. Single people walking on the road mostly wear "Good Citizen Certificates" on their chests, like government officials in the provincial capital wearing badges. There were no incidents of murder or robbery on the road. However, in the mountainous areas, there are still occasional remnants of bandits. During the bandit suppression period in the past, the upright gentry were either killed by the bandits or fled to other places to avoid disaster, and did not care about county affairs. The inferior gentry seized the opportunity to rise. At their peak, there were so-called "five pests" and "three evils." Now, they have slightly restrained their behavior, but the legacy they have left behind continues to poison society. In the countryside, whenever red bandits surrender, they are seen as an opportunity to get rich. Those with fields have their fields taken away, and those with houses have their houses taken away. Even the main culprits of murder and arson can rehabilitate themselves with money up to a dozen times, while those without money, even if they were coerced into following, are killed. It is difficult to eliminate the bandits, which is understandable. As for the current Lianbao (joint security) chiefs and Bao (village) chiefs, it is said that many of these people are mixed in among them. When the Bao chief travels, he is often escorted by two soldiers carrying guns. The authority of the Lianbao chief is even greater, and he is called the "土皇帝" (local emperor). The household registration fees collected vary from Bao to Bao. Some are divided into A, B, C, and D grades, with Grade A being four 角 per household, Grade B three 角, Grade C two 角, and Grade D one 角. Others are allocated according to household registration, and even the extremely poor cannot avoid paying. I don't know if the government has such regulations. (Dispatch from Yangxin, April 2nd)

Current Situation of the Levees in Zhongmu, Henan Province on the Yellow River - Stone Throwing for Reinforcement Can be Completed in Ten Days - 65

Kaifeng Dispatch: Wang Liren, Director of the River Affairs Bureau, accompanied by Zhang Guangcai, Chief of the Engineering Section, went to Zhongmu River to inspect the levees around 10 AM on the 16th, and returned to Bian that night. According to Wang, the peach blossom flood arrived three or four days ago, rising six 寸 (cun, unit of length) higher than usual. The levees built last year were significantly affected. According to the report from the Shangnan Sub-Bureau yesterday, the Dalian Top Rush in the 8th, 9th, and 10th fortresses of Shangfan in Zhongmu were due to continuous northwest winds and the breaking of waves. Wave action eroded the levee foundations and the old shoals. A total of 15 meters of rubble were used to reinforce the levee foundation of six levees in the 8th fortress, 16 meters of stones were used to reinforce the levee foundation of one levee in the 9th fortress, 8 meters of stones were used to reinforce the levee foundation of two levees, 30 meters of stones were used to reinforce the headwater stones of two levees in the 10th fortress, about 20 meters of stones were used to reinforce the headwater stones of three levees, and about 7 or 8 尺 (chi, unit of length) of stones were used to reinforce the headwater stones of four levees, with a height of about 1 公尺 (meter). During the inspection, orders were given to throw stones for reinforcement, with an estimated need of more than 500 and less than 1,000 方 (cubic meters) of stone, which can be completed in ten days. On the 17th, the water level was 2.04 meters at Shangnan, 1.53 meters at Xinan, 1.7 meters at Shangbei, and 1.14 meters at Xibei, completely at the same level. (Dated the 17th)

Anhui Province Implements Tea Export Registration - A Total of Seventeen Registration Offices Established in the Province - 66

Anqing Dispatch: During the tea sales season last year, the Department of Finance and Construction of Anhui Province jointly established tea export registration offices in the border areas of Anhui Province. This year, a portion of Qihong tea has been able to obtain tea loans based on the registration volume of last year. The government also supervised production and sales. Recently, with the Qingming Festival over, tea has been put on the market. The establishment of registration offices is imperative. However, due to the changes in the Qihong tea industry and local transportation, the location and organization of the offices should be slightly changed compared to last year. The tea business tax has already been finalized by the Department of Finance, with eleven offices established in: She County, Xiuyi, Qimen, Jingtai, Xuanlang, Tongshi, Taitong, Mabao (attached to Lianghekou Balitan), Maotan Factory, Huoshan (attached to Guanjia Ferry), and Qili River. Registration offices will be established simultaneously to inspect and collect taxes. It is expected that tax revenues will increase as a result. A table was prepared listing the organization and location of the registration offices and the expenses to be incurred, and registration measures were drafted and submitted to the provincial government for approval and implementation. A total of seventeen general and branch registration offices will be established in the province, such as: Wuhu, which governs the Lugang and Jinzhuge branch offices; Xuancheng, which governs the Wanzhi, Guangde, Xinhezhuang, and Langxi branch offices; Jiekou, which governs the Laozhuling branch office; Daohu, which governs the Daqiaotou branch office; Datong; Huaiyuan, which governs the Bengbu and Linhua branch offices; and Sanhe. The above locations will all establish tea trade export registration offices. When tea merchants pay business tax at the tea business tax bureau in the producing area, they should fill out and submit an application form, detailing the operator's name, store name, and other columns. The tax bureaus will immediately verify the merchants' application forms, and if there are no discrepancies, in addition to collecting taxes and issuing receipts as required, they will also fill out a tea merchant's notification and hand it over to the tea merchants for transport. When passing through each registration office, the receipt and notification should be presented to the registration office for verification and registration. Each registration office should compile a summary table at the end of each month and at the end of the term, summarizing the production and sales volumes, and submit it to the authorities for review along with the registration book. (Dated April 13th)

Problems of Learning (Part 2) 67

- Ai Wei, Dean of the School of Education, National Central University

The second relationship is the relationship between learning and emotions. We know that learning requires considerable intelligence, but if a person's emotions are unstable, it will be difficult to succeed in learning, even with intelligence. Examples of so-called emotional instability are given below:

Schools often hold speech and sports meetings, and participants all want to win the first-place prize. In fact, the purpose of schools holding these meetings is to give general students the opportunity to practice speaking, sports, and physical activity. However, for the sake of comparing skills, there are first and second place distinctions. Students should adopt the attitude that "victory and defeat are common in war." However, students are often arrogant when they win and resentful when they lose. Neither of these attitudes is very good. Winners should not be arrogant, and losers should not be resentful. Because failure is the mother of success, after failure, the cause of the failure should be investigated in order to improve. For example, even if one or two subjects fail in the graduation exam, we should often reread them afterward, and never worry all day long, thinking that this will never pass, and fearing that the next exam will also fail. This kind of attitude has a very large impact on academic performance. Students who are often worried are pessimistic about the world, and at the extreme, they become insane due to worry, or even commit suicide.

The second example of emotion is the emotion of love. Students are generally in their youth, and their bodies are well developed, so the emotion of love follows. The so-called "knowing good color means admiring the young and beautiful" is an inevitable fact. "Emotionally stable students interact with classmates of the opposite sex, learning from each other, as if nothing is happening. Even if they meet someone they like and talk about love, they will not forget to study. And because of mutual encouragement, their grades will be even better. However, those with unstable emotions are not like this. They fall in love at the slightest contact with the opposite sex, as if anyone is fit to be a spouse. When the other person responds with a cold shoulder, they hate them to the bone. After several such failures, they inevitably become a woman hater, and whenever they talk to friends about things involving women, they will scold women incessantly. This kind of 'fishing in the air' behavior is seen as ridiculous and pitiful by normal people. These people are truly the most emotionally unstable." Others include those who cannot delay reactionary impulses, that is, they want to get married as soon as they fall in love, regardless of their studies. We can draw the following principle: "Those who plan to continue their studies, if they have the opportunity to interact with the opposite sex, should not indulge in love, so as to avoid trouble. For example, middle school students who want to enter university or university students who want to continue their studies after graduation should prepare fully in middle school or university and should not become entangled in love and tie themselves in knots. This is for those with stable emotions. If emotions are not very stable, it is best to talk about marriage after completing their studies and becoming financially independent. If so, trouble can be avoided in life and academic work can be successful."

The third relationship is the relationship between learning and habits. If our habits are good, then learning progress will be fast. Otherwise, not only will progress be very slow, but it may also hinder learning.

There are many habits related to learning. The important ones are three, which are described below:

The first is the habit of honesty. Everyone knows the importance of this habit in general life. But is it not equally important in learning? The opposite of honesty is opportunism. Some students today lack the habit of honesty and instead use opportunistic methods. For example, they only count the years until graduation, regardless of whether they have gained any knowledge. Or, when taking exams, they are too concerned about gains and losses. When they enter the exam room and feel that the questions are too difficult, they claim to be sick and ask to withdraw, requesting a make-up exam later. Sometimes they avoid the difficult and take the easy. Before selecting a course, they will first inquire about the teacher's teaching methods. If there is a lot of practice required, the grading is very strict, and all the assigned reference books must be read, then they respectfully decline and leave as if they are about to be contaminated. Regarding the cultivation of the habit of honesty, we should nip it in the bud and prevent it from happening. "In the learning process, we should proceed step by step, and we must concentrate on it within a certain period of time. Only after learning is pure and skilled should we participate in the experiment. When taking an exam, answer the questions that can be answered, and leave the ones that cannot be answered blank. Do not answer something that is not asked in order to muddle through. If, unfortunately, we fail, then bury ourselves in reading until we fully understand it. In short, learning is for oneself, not for others. We only seek to understand ourselves, and we do not need to make others fully aware."

"Those who have an honest learning habit know themselves better and can decide in advance whether they are competent for the job, so they will not embark on it rashly, leading to failure afterward. In life, their mentality is more stable, unlike those who are dishonest and disregard their own facts, focusing on deceiving others. The difference between their words and actions is so great that it is like having a dual personality in a morbid state. Therefore, for the sake of physical and mental health, honesty is an indispensable habit in learning."

The second is the habit of order. If we usually adhere to order, it will be of great help in learning. For example, when listening to lectures and taking notes, if the notes are very organized, it can help with memory. Even if the notes taken during the lecture are very scribbled, if they are sorted out afterward, they will definitely be clear when the final exam comes. Many people do things perfunctorily. They seem to be able to recognize the unclear words at the time, but when they take them out to look at them two months later, they are completely unrecognizable.

The habit of order is a scientific habit. When we are doing experiments, if there is no order, the results will definitely be inaccurate. The habit of order is also an economical habit, because if everything is done in an organized manner and objects are taken and placed in an orderly manner, then doing the same thing every day will never lead to disorder. People without the habit of order put A here today and put it there tomorrow, so that they have to look for it every time they want to use it. Therefore, a lot of time is wasted, which is certainly uneconomical.

The third is the habit of perseverance. Perseverance is essential for learning, because academic work cannot be successful in a month or a year. It must be pursued throughout one's life until death. The so-called "it is never too old to learn." If scholars have no perseverance, progress will definitely be difficult. In schools, this habit of perseverance is easy to develop, because teachers guide them on weekdays, and the grades of each student are examined daily. At the same time, the goal is hung in front, and they cannot graduate without continuous effort. During the winter and summer vacations or after graduation, the habit of perseverance is easily destroyed, because there is no one to guide them at that time, and there is no goal, so they become lazy. At this time, we should cheer ourselves up and find ways to arouse our interest in reading. It is best to learn from each other with three or five classmates, because progress will be made with comparison. However, the plans before the vacation should not be too large. Trying to do too much often leads to nothing. We should also pay attention to this point.

The main idea of this article is based on my essay "Learning Hygiene." The sections in quotation marks are also taken from that essay. Readers who wish to do further research can read the Collection of Educational Psychology Essays (published by Zhonghua Book Company). - Author's postscript (End)

Several Hurricanes Cause Disaster in Wuhan - Three Towns' Brick Houses and Sheds Collapsed, Affecting 3,000 Households - Hundreds of Citizens Dead and Injured, Truly an Unprecedented Catastrophe 68

Hankou Dispatch: The atmospheric pressure here has been very low for the past two or three days, feeling extremely oppressive and hot, with the thermometer rising to seventy degrees. Unexpectedly, at 1:50 AM on the 18th, there was a sudden combination of thunder, lightning, and a fierce gust of wind, with all the apertures sounding. A torrential rain followed. The wind came from the northwest plateau and moved extremely fast, like ten thousand horses galloping, with roaring sounds. The power plant stopped the current supply due to precautions, and the entire city was dark, so only three people died from electric shock. The telephone was also out of service. After three hours, it finally cleared up, and the wind went straight along the Yangtze River towards the southeast. The business community here received a telegram from Sichuan on the evening of the 17th, saying that the hurricane had passed through eastern Sichuan at about 5:00 PM that day. Eight hours later, the wind reached Hankou. Fortunately, advance warnings had been received, prohibiting inland steamers from sailing. Moreover, the wind came late at night, so the losses on the river surface were small. Only one coal ship capsized in the Yangtze River at the Dadukou pier in Wuchang, and nine of the ten people on board drowned. In the two hours of storms in Wuhan, many houses collapsed and people were killed and injured. After the incident, investigations revealed that in Hankou, 86 brick houses collapsed on Zhongshan Road, Sanhuang Street, Huangpi Street, Minquan Road, Qianhualou, and Zhongzheng Road, killing 18 people and injuring more than 200. The most tragic were the poor people outside the railway who lived in sheds supported by bamboo mats. When the storms suddenly came, more than a thousand of these shacks had their bamboo mats blown away by the wind. Countless poor people were crying and calling for their parents and children in the storms, not knowing where to go. In addition, the sudden drop in temperature and shivering conditions were extremely miserable. In Wuchang, more than ten brick houses collapsed in Datongmen Kuaizi Street, Desheng Bridge, etc., killing 11 people and injuring dozens. The walls of the private residence of the Chairman of the Provincial Government, the Provincial Stadium, the Normal School, etc., were blown down by the wind. Two dormitories at Central China University collapsed, but fortunately no one was injured. Countless shacks along the river were blown away, leaving nothing behind. In total, three thousand households in the three towns of Wuhan had their brick houses and sheds blown down, and hundreds were killed and injured. This unexpected catastrophe is truly unbearable for the hard-pressed people. (Dated April 18th)

Expansion of Guangdong Provincial Textile Factory - The Sole Mission is to Revive the Silk Industry - The Various Departments in the Factory are on a Grand Scale 69

Guangzhou Dispatch: Since the implementation of the Three-Year Plan in Guangdong Province, no effort has been spared in the implementation of various industrial constructions. Industry construction is particularly emphasized. Since the three years, various provincial factories, such as textile factories, cement factories, sulfuric acid factories, caustic soda factories, beverage factories, paper mills, charcoal car furnace factories, fertilizer factories, sugarcane factories, and steel factories, have been established or expanded one after another. Guangzhou is becoming increasingly industrialized. Among them, the recent large-scale expansion and successive commencement of work of the provincial textile factory, at a time when the textile industry in our country is declining, is worthy of attention. Here is an exploration of its general situation:

Preparation Process

The Guangdong Provincial authorities, in view of the fact that the silk industry in this province has always been a major industry, but has been severely hit by foreign goods dumping and the impact of the global economic downturn, decided to establish a textile factory to rescue rural areas and revive the silk industry. It was approved by the 105th meeting of the 6th Guangdong Provincial Government in 1933, and immediately began to construct various factories, warehouses, and offices, and purchase various looms, generators, steam boilers, and all necessary machinery and equipment. It was further expanded in March 1934. Now, various departments have successively started construction, and the scale is grand, truly a great factory in South China.

Equipment Content

The factory site is located in Henan. The total area of the factory is 386,400 square feet. The factory is divided into silk weaving, silk reeling, spun silk linen yarn, wool spinning, cotton spinning, and electrical and mechanical departments, totaling six departments, covering an area of 217,884 square feet. The total area of other land is 386,400 square feet. The total capital is 5,147,076.66 yuan. The factory also built its own pond, which can supply the entire factory. The individual situations of each department can be described as follows: Silk Weaving Department: There are 60 looms, working ten hours a day, and each loom can produce 20 yards of silk. Later, due to the large increase in sales and insufficient supply, night shifts were added, and production can be doubled. Currently, the products include Nanxing crepe, Lizhi crepe, Huaguang crepe, silk serge, Yuehua crepe, wool crepe, modern twill, and Mingxing twill. The results are excellent. Silk serge is made entirely of Cantonese silk and is very popular among all sectors. For the purpose of expanding production, it was decided to purchase 100 looms. Silk Reeling Department: There are currently four silk reeling machines, totaling 142 cauldrons. On average, each cauldron produces 10 taels of silk per day. There are currently 200 trainees. During the training period, the daily output of silk is 260 taels. 150,000 catties of silkworm pupae are required each year. The produced raw silk is uniform. Multiple strands are reeled at 90 points, and sitting reeling is at 80 points. All products, with the silk weaving department's needs as the main product, and the remaining materials from silk reeling as by-products, can be used as spun silk raw materials. Spun Silk Linen Yarn Department: There are two refining cauldrons, one hemp steaming cauldron, one dehydrator, one hemp softening machine, four cotton interception machines, two first-pass carding machines, one each of second-pass carding machines, third-pass carding machines, and fourth-pass carding machines, four extension machines, three each of sliver making machines, roving making machines, and roving finishing machines, one combined sliver making and roving finishing machine, one 40-spindle coarse spinning machine, one 32-spindle coarse spinning machine, three 300-spindle fine spinning machines, one doubling machine, two twisting machines, two singeing machines, one yarn shaking machine, one baling machine, one Hans scale, one yarn twist testing machine, and one yarn testing machine, and 38 motors. The machinery in the Wool Spinning Department has been installed and a part has already started construction. The Cotton Spinning Department and the Electrical and Mechanical Department were completed at the end of last year, and have recently been put into operation.

News from the Bandit Suppression in Shanxi Province: The Bandits' Ranks Lack Arms and Ammunition, Putting Them in Dire Straits; The Yang Family Generals Display Extreme Bravery, Repeatedly Recapturing Famous Cities 70

Taiyuan Dispatch: The situation regarding bandit suppression in Shanxi Province has now turned from danger to safety. Concerning news snippets from the bandit areas and the rear, there are still some worth recording. I have gathered a few items below:

Playing Theater Everywhere: Whenever the bandits arrive at a place, if the National Army's pursuit is slightly slow, they immediately set up formations and stage their "red" theater to lure the people to watch and listen, taking the opportunity to carry out major propaganda. It is reported that they have done this kind of trick in Shuangchi Town in Lingshi County and Gucheng Town in Fencheng County.

Setting Off Paper Firecrackers: Although the Communist bandits who invaded Shanxi claim to number 30,000, their firearms are incomplete and dilapidated, and their quantity is extremely insufficient. Only about half of the entire group carries arms and ammunition. Recently, after being encircled and suppressed by the National Army on all sides, the bandits have suffered heavy losses. Because the river crossings along the Shanxi-Shaanxi border have all been blockaded by government troops, the bandits' supplies have long been cut off. Recently, due to a lack of ammunition, the bandits have been setting off paper firecrackers during nighttime battles with government troops to cover their movements.

Magistrate Seeking Guarantee: Although the bandits who invaded Shanxi are running around everywhere, encircling various county towns, none have actually been captured except for Xiangling. It was previously rumored that Hongdong City had fallen and the magistrate had died heroically, but this was actually a false rumor. After Xiangling County was captured, there were also many reports that Magistrate Kang Xiaomin had been killed. At that time, the government had even received such reports. Now, the county has been recovered, Kang is fortunately unharmed, and has already returned to his post. According to a letter from the county, Kang's survival was truly a matter of luck. After the bandits entered the city, they had already captured Kang, intending to put him to death immediately. However, because Kang had a good reputation and was highly praised by the people, the bandits asked the people whether Kang was a good official or a bad official. The people replied that he was a good official. The bandits then said that if he was a good official, he could be spared death if he could obtain a guarantee from twenty shops. The merchants were willing to vouch for Kang. After the guarantee forms from twenty shops were filled out, Kang was spared, taking the opportunity to hide in a business. However, the Chief of Public Security, Zhu Shiyu, was killed, which was indeed a matter of fortune and misfortune.

Main Reasons for the Bandits' Defeat: The main reasons for the bandits' defeat in attacking Shanxi are as follows: Yan Xishan has been preparing for communism for a long time. Although the county defense corps and police are not very effective in suppressing bandits, they have achieved considerable success in city defense work. The central government is extremely concerned about the bandit problem in Shanxi Province. Upon hearing the alarm, it mobilized a large army to take on the responsibility of defense, and sent Chen Cheng, the Chief of Staff of the Wuhan Headquarters, to Taiyuan, to reside there for a long period, assisting in the military affairs of suppressing the bandits. With such careful arrangements, victory could be achieved. The bandits lack arms and ammunition, and their strength has been further depleted in battles with the National Army. Judging from the recent situation, the bandits will surely become turtles in a jar. The people of Shanxi are inherently simple and honest, and rich in local ethical concepts. Although the bandits have been luring poor people everywhere to help them, judging from the situation in various counties that have been occupied by the bandits and then recovered, the people in various places have all stayed behind in their villages. Except for a very small number of local ruffians, few have worked for the bandits. Since they have lost the people, this is why they are bound to collapse.

The Yang Family Brothers: Among the senior generals of the Shanxi Army, there are four people with the surname Yang: Yang Aiyuan, Yang Chengyuan, Yang Yaofang, and Yang Xiaoou. Yang Aiyuan was originally a division commander. At the beginning of this war, he was appointed by Yan Xishan as the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression. Later, the central government sent a large army into Shanxi, and Chen Cheng was ordered to come to Taiyuan to assist in the suppression. Yan then reassigned Chen as the Commander-in-Chief of the First Route, and Yang as the Commander-in-Chief of the Second Route. Yang Chengyuan, Yang Xiaoou, and Yang Yaofang were all division commanders, and all participated in the war, personally directing operations. Yang Chengyuan's unit has been stationed in Linfen since 1930, responsible for guarding southern Shanxi, for several years. This time, Yang was ordered to lead his troops to attack the bandits in Xi County, but Linfen County, where his headquarters was located, was surrounded by bandits. Before long, Yang's hometown, Xiangling County, was also occupied by bandits. Yang's subordinates were extremely angry. Therefore, when the order to attack was issued, they cheered wildly. In less than a day and night, they charged and killed, fighting to Linfen, immediately relieving the siege of the county town. After a brief deployment, they rushed straight to Xiangling, and in a few hours, they recaptured Xiangling. They are truly brave. Furthermore, because Yang Aiyuan and Yang Chengyuan have the same surname and the same character "yuan" in their names, outsiders often suspect that they are brothers. In fact, Aiyuan's ancestral home is Wutai, and Chengyuan's ancestral home is Xiangling, one in the south of Shanxi and the other in the north of Shanxi, separated by a thousand miles.

Shooting Bandit Scouts: In their operations, the Communist bandits dispatched a large number of bandit scouts to lurk in various places to spy on the National Army's military situation. According to Yan Xishan's recent statement, as many as 5,000 of these bandit scouts have already entered Shanxi. Their tricks are truly appalling. In order to eliminate these people and reduce the eyes and ears of the bandits, the authorities ordered the relevant military, police, and constitutional organs in the provincial capital and the county troops and county governments to strictly arrest them. If there is solid evidence, they are allowed to execute them first and report later, in order to facilitate military operations. A Bandit Suppression Enforcement Office was specially established in the provincial capital to specifically try these bandit scout criminals. After this order was issued, executions were endless throughout the province. In the past few days, the provincial capital executed two or three bandit scouts at the execution ground outside the South Gate around noon every day, as a warning to those who work for the bandits. There were even two or three cases every day. Until recently, this trend has subsided slightly. It is reported that many have also been executed in other counties. According to reports received by the government, thirty-four people have already been executed in eight counties, including Yangcheng in eastern Shanxi. These counties are still not bandit areas, so what is happening in other counties can be imagined.

Change of County Magistrates: Since the rise of the bandit suppression campaign, many county magistrates have been replaced. Some have been dismissed for dereliction of duty, and some have resigned due to timidity. Among those who resigned, some feigned illness, some begged for mercy, and some used other methods or means. Therefore, the county magistrates who have been replaced in the past two months include those in Qi County, Lingshi, Anyi, Jiaocheng, Xinjiang, Puzhou, Fangshan, and Jiexiu, which is quite a few. (April 16)

Superintendent of the Ouhai Customs, Xu Hongbin: Second Inspection of the Patrol Team – Delivers Earnest Speech to Team Members – 71

Wenzhou Dispatch: Since taking office, Xu Hongbin, Superintendent of the Ouhai Customs, has spared no effort in reorganizing customs affairs. Recently, Xu noted reports that unscrupulous merchants in Fujian Province have established large-scale smuggling organizations. As Ouhai is adjacent to Fujian, Xu is deeply concerned about being affected. In addition to repeatedly writing to the Customs Department to instruct subordinates to pay close attention and take strict precautions, Xu believes that the customs patrol team is the key to suppressing smuggling. He conducted an inspection of the team in January and after several months, he conducted a second inspection at 11 a.m. on the 13th, accompanied by Tax Commissioner Ma and Assistant Qiao, at Jiangxin Islet. The team's various performances were impressive, and Xu delivered an earnest speech, which was photographed and distributed. It is reported that the Inspector General of Customs, impressed by Xu's attention to smuggling suppression, has transferred an Englishman named Mian Yan from the Kowloon Customs in Guangdong to train the Ouhai Customs patrol team. This Englishman has served as a naval officer in his country and has extensive experience in dealing with smuggling. He will train the team in Ouhai for a month. In the future, the results of smuggling suppression will surely improve, demonstrating Xu's and Inspector General Mei's attention to Ouhai Customs affairs. The following is an excerpt from Xu's speech during the inspection of the patrol team: "The patrol team is the key to the customs' smuggling suppression efforts. Everything about it is closely related to the future of customs affairs. The customs jurisdiction is vast, with many ports. I previously went to inspect the coastal areas, and drew up a plan to reorganize smuggling suppression efforts, which was submitted and adopted. The reason for this diligent effort to reorganize is that national taxes are the lifeblood of the country. To increase national taxes, we must strictly seize smuggled goods. The presence of smuggled goods not only harms national revenue but also hinders the business of legitimate merchants, which is extremely detrimental. On the customs side, the patrol team is the one that directly carries out the task of suppressing smuggling. Therefore, your responsibilities are very important. The strictness of your discipline, the cultivation of your character, and the progress of your smuggling suppression methods are all closely related to national tax revenues. Moreover, reports indicate that unscrupulous merchants in Fujian Province have recently organized large-scale smuggling companies, even setting up small radio stations to report the locations of customs patrol boats and various information such as returning to port, adding coal, and adding water. They have also built dozens of sailing ships for smuggling purposes. The situation is very serious. Our region is connected to Fujian Province and is bound to be affected. Therefore, I hope that you will redouble your efforts and patrol diligently, so as to eliminate smuggling and increase national tax revenues. This is what I strongly hope for, and I expect you to have good results."

Fengxian: Investigation of a Smoking Dispute 72

A resident of this county named Jin Fa, over fifty years old, smoked opium due to illness. After the government strictly prohibited opium last year, he obtained a license according to regulations. However, on the night of the 12th of this month, while he was smoking at the Songji smoking den in the town, Yu Yi, a newly arrived service member from the Public Security Bureau, a native of Jintan, came to investigate. Yu slapped him several times, injuring his brain. That night, he developed symptoms of insanity, drooling, with hemiplegia, and complete loss of consciousness. Doctors were helpless. On the 16th, swelling and redness appeared on his left ear and cheek, and thick liquid flowed from the orifice. He is on the verge of death, with no hope of survival. His son, Qi Wu, has already submitted a complaint to the county government, requesting punishment for the perpetrator, but there has been no result.

Suzhou: County Government Sends Commissioners to Strictly Collect Land Rent 73

The Wu County government, due to the fact that the farmers in Wu County have been claiming disaster and crop failure for the 24th year of the Republic, and tenants in Xiangcheng and other villages have even resisted paying rent, resulting in a harvest of less than 50%, has specially formulated a method for collecting rent. The discounted price should not exceed seven yuan and five jiao. Those with severe disasters are allowed to defer 20% of the payment. Zhang Yijun, Pan Renxian, and others have been appointed as rent collection commissioners and will go to collect rent today (20th). All payments must be made before the end of May. Those who are overdue will be detained and forced to pay. The local public security police are also instructed to provide assistance at any time in order to ensure the collection of rent.

All Circles Mourn Fei Zhongshan 74

The Wu County Chamber of Commerce, Suzhou Electric Factory, Suzhou Orphanage, and ten other groups and organizations initiated a memorial service for Fei Shuwei (Zhongshan) yesterday (19th) at 2 p.m. at the Fei residence in Taohuawu. Zhang Yipeng, Cheng Ganqing, County Magistrate Deng, and representatives from all walks of life attended. Zhang Yipeng and others reported on the significance of the memorial service, and the event ended around 5 p.m.

Wuxi: Strict Prohibition of Copper Coins Entering the City 75

The seventeen trade associations in this county, including wine, soy sauce, and tobacco, previously reported that the exchange rate of copper coins in Wuxi was uneven, with large fluctuations, causing significant losses to merchants and residents. They have already submitted a request to the provincial and county authorities to investigate and ban the practice, and have also requested the Ministry of Finance to instruct the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications to collect and exchange coins in accordance with the law. However, recently, copper coins from other areas have been entering the city, and speculative merchants are profiting from it. Yesterday, they submitted another request to the county government, requesting that a notice be issued to strictly prohibit the entry of such coins. If anyone is found carrying more than the legal amount, the public should be allowed to report them and confiscate the coins as a reward, in order to warn the offenders.

Appeal for Reduction of Rickshaw Tax 76

There are a total of 2,714 rickshaws in this county, of which only 1,759 are in the urban area, while 455 are in the rural area. Traditionally, each rickshaw paid a monthly local public welfare donation, which was originally one yuan, and then an additional sanitation donation of two jiao. Since the unified operation of urban and rural rickshaws in the autumn of the 21st year of the Republic, a public welfare donation of five jiao has been added, reducing five fen in the summer of the 22nd year. In total, each month each is one yuan and six jiao and five fen. Recently, the business tax bureau has repeatedly urged the payment of business tax, resulting in a heavy burden on small rickshaw owners. In Shanghai, Suzhou, Changzhou, and other places, rickshaws only pay a local monthly donation and there is no business tax. Only Zhenjiang, the provincial capital, levies business tax. However, before the business tax was levied, the local monthly donation was one yuan and four jiao. After the business tax was levied, the original monthly donation was reduced to one yuan. There is also a precedent to follow. Yesterday, the rickshaw industry sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce, requesting that it forward a letter to the county government, urging the removal of the original sanitation donation of two jiao, in order to alleviate the heavy burden.

Jiangyin: Jiangnan Steamer Allows Berthing at Wharf 77

The county chamber of commerce, in order to prosper the market, has negotiated with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to allow steamers to berth at the south bank for a trial period of six months. However, due to unresolved lease negotiations for the opening of the Kailuan Wharf, there have been obstacles. Wu Shouying and others from the Chamber of Commerce have entrusted Ji Xiangji to go to Shanghai to discuss with Liu Hongsheng, manager of Kailuan. They have agreed to lease the wharf location, and a contract will be signed next week. The Jiangnan steamer can then dock on the south bank.

Villagers Fight Over Opera Performance 78

Chenjia Village in Yunting, Second District, put on a Shaoxing opera performance, attracting nearby villagers, men and women, like a sea of people. A person from Jinjia Village shouted insults, and the two sides clashed, using knives and iron rods as weapons, injuring Chen Jinsheng, Tao Zhizhao, Wu Zishan, and Tao Xingbang from Chenjia Village. Chen Jinsheng's life is in danger. The injured were sent to the Fuyin Hospital. The perpetrators, Jin Aqi and others, were detained by the merchant corps and reported to the county for investigation on the 17th.

Yangzhou: Villagers Beat the Bureau Chief 79

At about 10 a.m. on the 18th, Shu Guohua, director of the Jiangdu Construction Bureau, was surrounded by more than 200 villagers, women and children, led by Zhao Yuansan (75 years old), at the earthwork engineering office outside the West Gate. They demanded the land price for the requisitioned land and questioned why the money had not been issued after it had been received. Director Shu announced that the money had not been allocated and that he would be responsible for submitting a request to the county. If they did not believe him, they could go to the county to inquire. However, the crowd was clamorous. At first, they were willing to go to the county together, but then they said it was not necessary and shouted, "Beat him!" (referring to Shu), "Take straw rope and drag him through the streets!" For a moment, the crowd surged like a tide. Shu ordered the gates of the office to be closed, but the villagers broke them open. Shu then fled into the house, but the villagers destroyed the furniture and pulled down the houses. Fortunately, Shu escaped. He was still surrounded, but a few workers rushed to protect him. At the same time, the villagers knocked down the engineer Fan Jiliang, using a straw rope to pull his neck, and dragged him into the mud. At that time, most of the workers returned to the office for lunch and asked what was happening. The villagers attacked them without asking questions, breaking their heads. This aroused public anger, and they fought each other, as if facing an enemy. In the chaos, supervisor Ge Jiasheng and Shu Qifan, son of Director Shu, were injured. Zhao Yuansan's head was also broken. Liu Xianwen, captain of the 22nd Security Brigade, led the security team to suppress the situation, but there was no way to do so. Later, the workers gathered together and escorted Director Shu out of danger from the crowd. However, his jacket was torn and his hat was lost. He hurriedly took a car into the city to report the situation to acting County Magistrate Wang Jizhi and ask for instructions on how to deal with the aftermath. After discussion with the heads of the land and political affairs departments, they decided to report the situation to the Department of Finance and request the allocation of land prices. The northwest gates were temporarily closed to prevent villagers from entering the city. Zhang Shu, director of the Public Security Bureau, also led a special task force of 30 people out of the city to rescue Director Shu and persuaded the villagers to leave. By the time the security and special task forces entered the city, it was already late at night.

Ningbo: Preserving the Tombs of Local Worthies 80

The Yin County Literature Association believes that the tombs of local worthies in the urban and rural areas should be preserved to preserve historical sites and inspire admiration. At the 12th meeting on the 17th, it was decided to recommend Feng Tongsheng, Ye Youyi, Cai Ziqing, Zhang Yidong, Yang Juting, Feng Mengzhuan, and Chen Renxuan for review. The standard for protecting the tombs of worthies should be based on those listed in the biographies in the old and new county chronicles. Regarding the tombs of worthies that must be moved, the person in charge of the public cemetery should be notified to designate a duty area for proper burial. After the review is passed, the association will erect a sign and notify the local townships to protect it. A request should be submitted to the county government for approval and implementation.

Hangzhou: Wu Tingyang Inspects the Sea Dike 81

Wu Tingyang, Director of the Department of Construction, believing that the heavy rains in recent days have caused the Qiantang River to rise sharply and the sea dike is in danger, took a car to Haining and Haiyan to inspect the dangerous condition of the dike, accompanied by his secretary Yang Wenzhao. He returned to the province in the evening and plans to raise funds for repairs.

Xiaoshan: Nine-Year-Old Girl Burned to Death 83

Cao Weisheng from Shicun outside the South Gate of Xiaoshan built a grass hut in the official river to watch over the fish. Cao's nine-year-old daughter stayed there with her father every night. On the night of the 15th, Cao went out, leaving the girl to watch over the fish hut. Unexpectedly, the girl was young and ignorant. The oil lamp she lit overturned and spread to the fish hut. In an instant, the fire blazed fiercely. The girl and the fish hut were turned to ashes. The girl was charred and her face was burned. She fell into the river and died. The scene was terrible. When Cao returned, he pulled up the dead body, and wept bitterly.
