Local News

New Norwegian Minister to China, Mr. Kolban, Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning: Awaits Negotiations Before Setting Date to Proceed to the Capital 84

The newly appointed Norwegian Minister to China, concurrently the Minister to Siam and Japan, Mr. Kolban, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 7 a.m. to assume his post, accompanied by his wife. They arrived on the British company ship "Ranchi Putana", which arrived in Wusong the night before and entered the port yesterday morning. At about 7 a.m., it docked at the Jardine, Matheson Wharf on the Bund. Those who went to the ship to welcome him included Tang Shixuan, representing Mayor Wu Tiecheng; Zhang Mengling, representing the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs; Mr. Or, the Norwegian Chargé d'Affaires and Consul-General in Shanghai; Vice-Consul Kilde; Erwei; and many community leaders. After exchanging greetings with the welcoming party on the ship, Mr. Kolban and his wife disembarked at about 8 a.m. and went to the Astor House Hotel on the Bund to rest. They plan to visit Zhou Jun, the representative of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, this morning to discuss the presentation of his credentials and will also visit Mayor Wu.

Norwegian Minister Kolban and his wife (Photo by International Society)

Remarks: Mr. Kolban met with reporters from various newspapers on the ship and made the following remarks: "I have been transferred from my post as Minister to Portugal to become the Minister to your country, concurrently the Minister to Japan and Siam. I departed from Oslo, Norway on February 6th and spent ten days in Bangkok, Siam. After arriving in China, I originally planned to stay for two months, but due to the long delays en route, I have had to change my plans. I will only stay in China for a short time. After proceeding to the capital to present my credentials, I will return to Shanghai and take a ship to Japan. I will reside in Tokyo and wait until I have presented my credentials in Japan before returning to China. I plan to travel to various places and will travel between China, Japan, and Siam at any time. The date for proceeding to the capital to meet with Chairman Lin and present my credentials, as well as to visit Foreign Minister Zhang and other authorities, will be determined after further negotiations. I have spent a long time on the Pacific coast and have passed through Shanghai by ship, but I have never disembarked and set foot on your country's soil. This is my first time. The relationship between China and Norway is very strong and there are no disputes. I will strive to further improve it."

Mr. Kolban's Brief Biography

When Mr. Kolban arrived in Shanghai, he was wearing a grey tweed suit, yellow leather shoes, and glasses. His hair was already grey and his attitude was very amiable. He is 60 years old and a senior member of the Norwegian diplomatic service. He graduated from the University of Oslo in Norway. He first served as an attaché at the Norwegian Consulate General in Kobe, Japan, and was later promoted to Consul General in various cities, including British Australia. He was later promoted to Minister. In recent years, he has served as Minister to Portugal. After the previous Norwegian Minister to China, Japan, and Siam, Mr. Oberta, was transferred, the Norwegian government, believing that Mr. Kolban had previously resided in the Far East and was familiar with the Far East situation, transferred him to succeed Mr. Oberta. Because Mr. Kolban is a concurrent Minister, the Norwegian Consul-General in Shanghai, Mr. Or, will serve as Chargé d'Affaires during his absence. Mr. Or will also be returning to his country soon. The Norwegian government originally intended to assign Ministers to reside permanently in both China and Japan, but was unable to do so due to limited funds.

The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association's Stance on Anti-Smoking 86

The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association, with today being the closing day of the Shanghai Anti-Smoking and Anti-Drug Campaign Week, specifically issued a declaration, presenting the association's ten major proposals for anti-smoking. The original text is recorded as follows: 1. Opium is the primary cause of poverty and weakness, and the guiding thread of foreign aggression. For more than a century, it has created the current semi-colonial state. Internally, the people are impoverished and resources are exhausted; externally, strong neighbors are invading, creating a precarious situation that cannot last. It is truly as the ancient sages have shown us, "Things must first decay before insects breed," and "A country must first be attacked by itself before others attack it." All Chinese people should share this feeling and recognition. Throughout history, those who spoke of banning smoking, from Lin Zexu onwards, were in every generation. However, due to the disorganization of groups and the inadequacy of strength, evil often prevailed over good. It is painful to speak of. Since 1924, leaders from various groups and sectors in Shanghai, aware of the rampant disaster and the imminent demise of the country, initiated the National Anti-Drug Movement and organized the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association to take responsibility for its promotion. The call resonated throughout the country, and over 4 million people swore to join the anti-drug movement and requested the League of Nations to limit the world's production of drugs to scientific and medicinal uses. World opinion shifted, recognizing this as a sign that the Chinese people had awakened. Since then, anti-drug comrades in various places have made unremitting efforts to oppose the opium monopoly and protest forced opium cultivation. Many have sacrificed their lives as a result. Unfortunately, during the reign of warlords, the authorities only sought revenue, and the results were not significant. The disaster of smoking remained as before. Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, it has repeatedly responded to public requests and expressed its intention to ban smoking. However, due to internal troubles that have not yet been resolved and the failure of general administration to get on track, it is difficult to achieve practical results. In the past two years, government leaders have sensed the severity of the national crisis and realized that without starting with banning smoking, there will be no way to achieve rejuvenation and save the country from danger. Hence, the approval of the six-year smoking ban plan, extending from ten provinces to the whole country, from narcotic drugs to opium. Now, we feel even more the difficulty of banning smoking and the deep penetration of the disaster of smoking into society. Without the concerted cooperation of the government and the people, it will be difficult to achieve complete results. Therefore, this Anti-Smoking and Anti-Drug Campaign Week is being held, mobilizing all sectors of the party, government, military, and people to make a collective move against the disaster of drugs. It is expected that wherever the army goes, complete success will be achieved, and the century-old disaster of drugs will be completely eliminated, giving this ancient country, which is on the verge of death, a chance to revive. Then, this smoking ban will not be in vain. However, the major policy of banning smoking has countless threads and ends. The central government may not have the determination to completely ban it, and local areas may continue their old ways of outwardly complying but inwardly opposing. If strict enforcement is not carried out, it will be like building a mountain one basket at a time, only to give up halfway. Not only will the deadline for banning smoking be extended, but the spread of the disaster of smoking will become even more uncontrollable. Members of this association have been engaged in anti-drug work for twelve years and have a deep understanding of what they have seen and heard. We humbly present the following proposals, hoping that the leaders of the smoking ban will adopt and implement them, as it will be fortunate not only for the smoking ban, but also for the party and the country. Moreover, Shandong and Zhejiang provinces, as well as Qingdao and Nanjing cities, have implemented a policy of complete prohibition, and their results are better than those of other provinces and regions. It is hoped that this method will be promoted throughout the country to achieve the effect of early elimination. In many provinces, smoking bans are handled by contractors, who have established opium paste shops. Although on the surface, they are only for supplying the needs of registered smokers, in reality, they are expanding sales and using clever strategies. Some contractors openly formulate regulations that only allow opium paste shops to sell more opium paste, not less, as a standard for reward and punishment. The authorities should strictly prohibit this situation to prevent abuses. There are many merchants who sell opium soil on consignment in various places, colluding with local officials and foreign rogues, taking advantage of special forces to smuggle private soil for personal gain and profit from drugs. Before the opium paste shops are eliminated, the government should pay attention to this. In South China and North China, under the protection of [blanks in original], rogue smugglers of drugs are openly unbridled. The government should quickly [blanks in original] effective measures to stop them, so as not to [blanks in original] the opportunity to create sales of drugs by banning smoking. The so-called front door rejects the tiger, and the back door lets in the wolf. The result will be even more uncontrollable. It is hoped that the government will allocate all smoking ban revenue to the expenses of smoking cessation, anti-drug propaganda, and anti-drug education, both to make remedial arrangements and to prevent the disaster of drugs before it happens, so as to achieve the goal of permanent prohibition. It is hoped that the government will [blanks in original] in remote opium-growing provinces, such as Yunnan, Guizhou, Sichuan, Shaanxi, Gansu, Ningxia, Chahar, and Suiyuan, regions where opium seedlings have not yet been eradicated, order farmers to switch to growing cotton and grains from this year onwards, and completely ban planting early, so as to cut off the source and eliminate the disaster of drugs. The government has taken resolute action in banning highly toxic drugs, but private manufacturing and selling still exist everywhere. The reason for this is that the raw materials used to manufacture drugs are not managed, and they are readily available in pharmacies everywhere. The government should pay attention to this. We ask the government to cooperate with the League of Nations and the governments of various countries to cancel the opium monopoly imposed on overseas Chinese in various colonies in Southeast Asia within a time limit. We ask the Ministry of Education to order all levels of schools to increase the use of special anti-drug teaching materials. The government should cooperate effectively with the people and social organizations in strictly enforcing the smoking ban, so as to assist where the law cannot reach and achieve the actual effect of prohibition.

The Yellow River: Closed One Month Early, Autumn Harvest Increased by 50 Million Yuan, Public Bonds Pledged at Only 1% Interest 87

Chairman Kong Xiangrong of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission came to Shanghai to meet with Minister Kong to request instructions on unified river defense measures, and also met with Standing Committee Members Sun and Song of the Economic Commission to present everything. This time, the closing and joining of the embankments was completed one month ahead of schedule, before the Qingming Festival, with the river flow cut off. From an agricultural perspective, this is of great importance. The crops planted in the provinces along the river, such as corn, sorghum, and soybeans, are all sown in April and May, and the Qingming Festival is the beginning of cultivation. After this, a bumper harvest is difficult to expect, or the entire year may be wasted. Taking this Yellow River disaster as an example, the area of the disaster area is estimated to be 10,000 square kilometers, equivalent to about 16 million mu. Excluding mountains, lakes, and houses, with 10 million mu, and each mu yielding a minimum price of five yuan, the autumn harvest of crops can be worth more than 50 million yuan. Moreover, the people can return to their fields and will not become bandits, which is also of great benefit politically. It is also reported that the 3 million yuan in public bonds for the Dongzhuang Yellow River closing project were pledged to seven banks, including the Jinan Central Bank, for 1.5 million yuan in cash, with a monthly interest rate of only 1%, which is offset by the interest on the public bond notes, and there are no prepaid discounts or anything else, which shows the enthusiasm of the banks in providing assistance.

Sun Ke Discusses the Draft Constitution, Adding Transitional Clauses, Necessary to Authorize the President to Issue Emergency Decrees, Fiscal Problems in Extraordinary Times are Academic Views 89

Various parties have been discussing the addition of transitional clauses to the draft constitution in recent days. The New Voice Agency reporter visited President Sun Ke of the Legislative Yuan at his private residence on Columbia Road yesterday afternoon to inquire about everything. We were granted an audience, and the following is a record of Sun's remarks: According to Sun, the addition of [blanks in original] clauses to the draft constitution was discussed yesterday (the 18th) by the Constitution Draft Review Committee, and will be submitted to the Standing Committee for further discussion in the middle of the week. As for its content, [blanks in original] such as the provisions of the constitution that the county magistrate is elected by the people, but in counties where local autonomy has not been completed, it is difficult to elect the county magistrate by the people. Therefore, a transitional measure must be stipulated: In counties where local autonomy has not been completed, the county magistrate shall be temporarily appointed by the government, and then elected by the people after local autonomy is completed. As [blanks in original] legislative members and supervisory members, it is also stipulated that they are elected by the people. However, according to the current actual situation, there must also be a transitional measure, that is, some are elected by the people, and some are temporarily appointed by the government, and then fully elected by the people when the time is right. [blanks in original] Regarding the issue of the implementation of the constitution, whether it should be implemented immediately after promulgation, or whether a transitional period should be stipulated, and implemented after a considerable period of time after promulgation, etc., all remain to be discussed.

Authorizing the President to Issue Emergency Decrees

Regarding the authority of the President to issue emergency decrees, Sun explained that this is common in Europe and the United States. For example, in France, for the franc problem, the parliament temporarily passed a case authorizing the President to take emergency measures at any time to stabilize finance. Also, the United States' economic recovery policy was authorized by Congress to the President to act expediently. China is facing internal and external troubles. In the event of an emergency, if normal procedures are followed, the National Assembly must be convened, and the matter must be resolved by the Assembly, then the event will have passed. Therefore, there must be a provision authorizing the President to issue emergency decrees, so that in the event of an emergency, the President can take appropriate action, and then follow normal procedures and submit it to the National Assembly for ratification.

Additional Representatives from the Northeast Awaiting Discussion

After the Constitution Draft was revised by the Central Constitution Draft Review Committee on the 18th, it must be passed by the Standing Committee on the 23rd, and then submitted to the Legislative Yuan for revision and collation. The draft will then be completed. On May 5th, the Central Government will formally announce the draft, and then it will be submitted to the National Assembly for approval and promulgation. The election of the President and other issues will have to await discussion and decision by the National Assembly. As for the generation of representatives to the National Assembly, the five provinces and cities in the Northeast requested an increase in the number of representatives they occupy, which is too small. Whether the Central Government will accommodate this request remains to be decided by the Standing Committee.

No Objections from the Southwest to Participate

Recently, consultations with Wang Liangchou, Dai Jitao, Ye Chuzhen, and others also concerned the draft constitution. Wang contributed his opinions as a jurist and did not represent Mr. Hu Hanmin. The comrades in the Southwest have no objections to the addition of transitional clauses to the draft constitution. As for the time of Mr. Hu's arrival in the North, as I have not obtained accurate information, I have not met with Cheng Tianzhou recently, so I am sorry for not being able to tell you everything.

Fiscal Problems in Extraordinary Times

Regarding fiscal problems in extraordinary times, according to Sun, this is the academic view of Ma Yinchu and other scholars, not the proposal of the Finance Committee under the Legislative Yuan. However, in my opinion, in the future, the income tax will be the main source of national fiscal revenue, but it will be difficult to compare with European and American countries in our economically backward country. Therefore, this kind of academic view seems to be difficult to allow in practice.

Measures for Receiving New Banknotes from Various Banks Have Been Determined 90

According to the Guowen News Agency, the Preparatory Committee for the Issuance of Banknotes of the Ministry of Finance previously received inquiries from the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications about how to handle the new banknotes that have been printed but not yet issued among the guarantee reserves of the eight issuing banks. The Preparatory Committee immediately forwarded a letter to the Ministry of Finance for inquiry. It is now heard that the handling method has been determined, that is, when receiving the new banknotes that have been printed but not yet issued by the various banks, the various expenses incurred when printing them abroad will be deducted from the cash reserves in full. For example, if a certain bank issues banknotes and must pay 4,000 yuan in cash and 6,000 yuan in bonds for every 10,000 yuan, if the bank has 50,000 new banknotes that have been printed but not yet issued, and the printing cost is 2,000 yuan, then when receiving them, all the new banknotes will be taken and sealed, and the printing cost of 2,000 yuan will be used to offset the cash certificate of 4,000 yuan, and another 2,000 yuan in cash will be paid.

Chairman's Report

Following the customary protocol, Chairman Zhou Xuexiang delivered a report, stating that the term of the third session's executive and supervisory committee members had long expired. According to the union's organizational law, elections should have been held last spring, but due to the nation's troubles and the severity of the situation, the elections were postponed by order of the Party Headquarters until today, when the fourth delegates' congress was convened. The number of representatives attending today exceeds that of previous sessions, and their punctuality fully demonstrates the deep understanding of responsibilities and future directions among our labor circles. In addition to aligning labor circles' steps, strengthening unity, and maximizing the function of collective organizations, we must all recognize the great difficulties facing us and, under the leadership of Chairman Chiang, make our utmost efforts for the national salvation movement and the revival of China. With the current bankruptcy of industry and commerce and the increasing unemployment, the suffering endured by our city's workers is rapidly intensifying. To resolve the issue of livelihoods, we must first focus on flourishing industry. Therefore, we must enhance production efficiency and, with a spirit of diligent hard work, pave a path for national industry to thrive. He hoped that all representatives attending today would jointly shoulder this responsibility.

Union Affairs Report

Standing committee member Shao Xubai then represented the third session's executive and supervisory committee in reporting on the general state of affairs, stating that the third session's executive and supervisory committee had originally planned many work projects, with a particular focus on the construction of labor movement undertakings. However, due to limited finances, significant difficulties were encountered in implementation. Furthermore, due to the limited capabilities of the committee members, significant contributions were not made, for which he expressed deep regret to the representatives. He then provided a brief report on the most important work of the third session. In terms of organization, the union has reviewed and issued membership certificates to 98 labor unions throughout the city, totaling over 160,000 members as of recently. While some unions have faced stagnation due to factory closures and member unemployment, the majority of unions have been able to maintain unified intentions and synchronized progress. Regarding labor-capital disputes, the union has made every effort to prevent them before they occur. In 1935, 34 cases were resolved through union mediation (cases not mediated by the union were not included in the statistics). Significant cases included the cancellation of uncompensated leave at the Yixin Toothbrush Factory, the closure of the Minsheng Yarn Factory, the opposition of Zhabei Water and Electricity Company workers to service regulations, the dismissal of workers at the Shenxin Yarn Factory, and the Xiangtai Timber Firm contracting incident. However, the causes of disputes in various industries largely stemmed from employers suspending operations, reducing wages, or dismissing workers, with no disputes arising from worker demands for improved treatment or increased wages. This demonstrates that the city's labor circles have been able to deeply understand the current difficulties and implement labor-capital cooperation. In terms of worker welfare, in addition to striving to oversee the establishment of literacy schools by various unions, six labor supplementary night schools were also established. According to recent statistics, over 1,000 male and female workers are enrolled. Originally, it was intended to add more schools in each district, but this could not be achieved due to financial constraints. (4) Regarding publicity work, the session revived the Shanghai Labor Monthly, changing it to a semi-monthly publication and then to a weekly publication. Special issues were also published on Labor Day last year and on National Day. However, after the fourteenth issue, it was forced to cease publication due to financial difficulties. Other matters, such as participating in emergency relief efforts, jointly addressing the North China autonomy issue with various sectors, requesting central government relief for unemployment, and handling daily union affairs, will not be reported in detail due to time constraints. Liu Xinquan then reported on the detailed conditions of various labor schools, in brief.

Instructions from Higher Authorities

Following the report, Lu Jingshi, representative of the City Party Headquarters, delivered instructions, stating that the large number of attendees today and their vibrant spirit were deeply gratifying. The past work of the General Labor Union, thanks to the efforts of all executive and supervisory committee members, has achieved remarkable success and is highly commendable. Although the organization of the General Labor Union has no legal basis, the various committees have been able to maintain it through hard work, and the Party Headquarters has filed it for record. The central government is also expected to approve the filing soon. He hoped that after obtaining legal status in the future, particular attention should be paid to: (1) Building economic strength. The advancement of any undertaking depends on the soundness of the economic organization. The General Labor Union's weak economic situation has hindered the development of union affairs. It is hoped that all labor unions in the city will take more responsibility. (2) Striving to train workers. The nation is facing severe difficulties, reaching a critical point. The General Labor Union should earnestly focus on promoting training, so that workers have a genuine understanding of the nation and the people, which can unleash great strength. (3) Strictly abiding by discipline. All workers in the city should unanimously obey the labor union, abide by resolutions, and obey the orders of the Party, strictly adhering to Party discipline. Only then can unity be strengthened. He hoped that everyone could work together to achieve these points.

Election of Executive and Supervisory Committee Members

The election of the fourth session's executive and supervisory committee members followed. The list of elected members is as follows: Executive Committee members: Zhu Xuefan, Zhou Xuexiang, Ye Xiangyuan, Shao Xubai, Li Mengnan, Long Peiyun, Shui Xiangyun, Fan Yifeng, Li Hua, Zhang Linhua, Chen Xiupu, Chuan Dewei, Zhao Zhenhui, Zhang Yiping, Zhou Qigui, Zhang Kechang, Ding Changyan, Hu Menglin, Yu Ting; Alternate Executive Committee members: Zhang Yuanming, Zou Dexin, Lu Muqin, Yu Yaoqiu, Le Junwen, Ying Yukang, Chai Zhenyou, Yan Quanrong, Zhang Shanqin. Passed Proposals

The following important proposals were then passed: (1) Proposal for raising funds to purchase an airplane for birthday greetings. (2) Proposal for sending a telegram of condolences to Chairman Chiang. (3) Proposal for submitting a request to the central government to amend Articles 20 and 21 of the Labor Union Law. (4) Proposal for submitting a request to the central government to instruct the Judicial Yuan to issue a directive to all levels of courts nationwide, stating that in the event of factory or store bankruptcy, employees' compensation rights should be given priority. (5) Proposal for all workers in the city to consistently practice labor-capital cooperation, strive to intensify production, develop national industry, and build the national economy. (6) Proposal for organizing the second city-wide workers' sports congress and actively promoting worker sports. (7) Proposal for actively promoting labor education to improve workers' knowledge. (8) Proposal for preparing a grand celebration to commemorate the upcoming May 1st Labor Day. (9) Proposal for sending a letter of condolences in the name of the congress to the union chairman, Zhu Xuefan, who has been appointed as the Chinese labor representative to the upcoming International Labor Conference, urging him to strive for breakthroughs and bring honor to our country. (10) Proposal for issuing a congress declaration.

Telegram to Chairman Chiang

The congress sent a telegram of condolences to Chairman Chiang, which read: To Chairman Chiang of the Nanjing Military Commission: Since your leadership of the revolution, you have been diligently striving and loyal to your goals. Your great achievements are worthy of being recorded for eternity. Your prestige is overflowing, surpassing the past and illuminating the present. Now, with the increasing urgency of foreign invasion and the deepening national crisis, you, sir, do not hesitate to endure hardship and preside over the central government. With unwavering spirit, you bury yourself in hard work for the nation. The New Life Movement is advancing, showing the beginnings of China's revival. Economic construction gives the people hope of recovery. Sincerity can move even metal and stone, and the entire nation responds. This congress dares to lead 800,000 workers in Shanghai to offer our sincere support and unanimous endorsement. We respectfully send this telegram of condolences, our hearts full of admiration. Zhu Xuefan, Zhou Xuexiang, Li Mengnan, Chairman Presidium of the Fourth Congress of the Shanghai General Labor Union, Secretary-General Shao Hubai, and all representatives bow in unison.

Congress Declaration

The fourth delegates' congress issued a declaration, which read: This union was established in the autumn of grave national crisis after the September 18th Incident. Entrusted with the heavy responsibilities by the city's labor circles and the earnest expectations of society, we deeply recognize the mistakes of past labor movement policies. The results of class struggle have only dealt a major blow to China's fragile industry and commerce, nipping them in the bud. We also deeply realize that under the constant aggression of the powers, Chinese workers, to seek genuine liberation, must first take the development of national capital and the prosperity of national industry as prerequisites. In the meantime, we must closely organize and concentrate our forces, follow the teachings of the late Dr. Sun Yat-sen, and under unified and strengthened unity, eliminate the shackles of unequal treaties imposed by various countries and seek the overall revival of the Chinese nation. We, the members of this union, are mindful of the magnitude of the mission we shoulder and strive diligently, not daring to be negligent. However, due to the difficult environment and our own insufficient capabilities, we have achieved few significant results over the past five years. This is something that we, as members, have been deeply ashamed and regretful of. Today, the difficulties are even deeper, and the foreign threats are even more urgent. Coupled with the extreme panic of the global economy and the compounding of natural disasters and human calamities, industry and commerce are on the verge of bankruptcy. When we look back on the past and look forward to the future, we deeply feel that our responsibilities cannot be shirked, and we can only strive diligently under the leadership of the Party and follow Chairman Chiang's instructions to work hard, work quickly, and work practically. Now, at the time of the fourth delegates' congress, we dare to present three things as the goals of our future endeavors: (1) Promote practical labor-capital cooperation and intensify production to develop national industry. Shanghai is the center of the nation's industry and commerce. Since the January 28th Incident, the market has been depressed, and all industries have been struggling, which is an undeniable fact. In addition, with the massive dumping of foreign goods, major industries such as silk, yarn, silk fabrics, cotton, rubber, and tobacco have experienced factory closures and wage reductions one after another. Under these critical circumstances, workers are enduring the pain of their livelihoods being on the verge of collapse, and employers deeply feel the difficulty of maintaining operations. To break through this difficult situation, we must passively avoid pointless labor-capital disputes and actively promote practical cooperation between labor and capital. Under mutual understanding, we will diligently bury ourselves in hard work together, improve technology, intensify production, and reduce the cost of production as much as possible to compete with foreign goods. Only then can national industry rely on growth and development, and the suffering of workers can be truly alleviated. (2) Promote worker sports and strengthen workers' physiques. Gu Yanwu once said, "The rise and fall of a nation is the responsibility of every individual." Today, our country is facing endless internal and external troubles. At this critical moment for the nation's fate, we cannot forget our responsibilities to the nation and the people. To shoulder this significant responsibility, we must first have a healthy physique, and only then can we be able to endure hardship, bear heavy burdens, and go far. Therefore, in the future, this union will actively promote worker sports and physical training, so that the physical and mental well-being of ordinary workers can be fully developed, and they can use the spirit of self-improvement to create vitality for the nation. (3) Promote labor education and improve workers' knowledge. Chinese workers have been despised by the general public due to their low level of education. Furthermore, due to their shallow knowledge and thought, they are easily taken advantage of. To raise the status of workers, we must prioritize improving workers' knowledge. Therefore, in addition to actively promoting labor education to eliminate labor illiteracy, we must also pay attention to the widespread implementation of training, cultivate workers' habits of collective living, and cultivate the foundations of social organization. The above three points are not just limited to these, but encompass a wide range of meanings. We will not make empty declarations, nor dare to boast. We will adhere to these principles and exert our efforts to achieve them. We hope that the Party and government authorities and social leaders will strictly supervise, provide assistance, and that all workers will be united in their efforts to complete this important mission. This declaration is made here.

Seafarers' Party Headquarters and Others Hosted a Banquet Yesterday for Zhao and Zhu, Two Representatives Attending the Geneva International Labor Conference 92

Zhao Banfu, design committee member of the Chinese Seafarers' Special Party Headquarters, has been appointed by order of the Central Government as a representative to attend the Geneva International Maritime Conference. He is scheduled to depart on the 24th of this month with Zhu Xuefan, the representative attending the International Labor Conference. The Chinese Seafarers' Party Headquarters and Union, together with representatives from seafarer associations such as the China Merchants Wharfingers' Association, Yan Ying General Office, Commercial Shipping Joint Benefit Association, Ewo Wharfingers' Club, New Taikoo Club, and Zhongcang Association, held a banquet at the Tao Le Chun Restaurant yesterday in honor of the two representatives. The attendees included representatives Zhao and Zhu, as well as Cheng Haifeng, director of the International Labor Bureau. The details are as follows:

Mr. Liu's Speech

First, Mr. Liu of the Seafarers' Party Headquarters delivered a speech, stating that today marks the eve of Representatives Zhao and Zhu's departure overseas. He wished to say a few words on behalf of his seafarer comrades. He felt that seafarers were also a type of worker, but workers worked on land, while seafarers worked on water. The prosperity of a nation is often directly proportional to the length of its coastline, and the length of the coastline is closely related to the number of seafarers. Therefore, the advance or decline of seafarers and their numbers have a profound relationship with the nation, the people, national defense, the military, industry, agriculture, and commerce. Our clothing, food, housing, and transportation, except for natural products, are all indebted to the benevolence of workers. However, the low wages, unequal treatment, and difficult and arduous conditions of our country's workers are truly unbearable to witness. We hope that when Representatives Zhao and Zhu attend the international conference this time, they will convey the suffering of all Chinese workers to the international community. There are many issues that need to be raised, but the most crucial are the following two: (1) Improving the status of workers. (2) Relieving the suffering of workers. Only in this way can we live up to our late Dr. Sun Yat-sen's legacy of actively seeking happiness for workers. He now drank a full cup, wishing them a smooth journey. Wang Jiyi, secretary of the Seafarers' Union, then delivered a speech, stating that the welfare and treatment of seafarers are not only their own problems, but also the demands of the entire nation. Workers of weak and small nations, facing meager wages and unequal treatment, should naturally strive to alleviate their suffering. He hoped that Representatives Zhao and Zhu would take advantage of this international conference to make a comprehensive request and also find time to make connections in order to obtain assistance in economic, spiritual, and material terms and to promote the plight of weak and small nations in order to awaken nations that treat us equally. He drank this cup to celebrate.

Mr. Zhu's Reply

Zhu Xuefan replied, stating that he was very grateful for the banquet hosted by the Chinese Seafarers' Party Headquarters, the Seafarers' Union, and various associations. He said that his knowledge and experience were very shallow, and he had no confidence in the outcome of attending the International Labor Conference by order of the Central Government. He sincerely accepted the good advice given by Mr. Liu and Mr. Wang and was willing to work with Representative Zhao to do his best to achieve a satisfactory outcome at the Labor Conference and the Maritime Conference. He knew that the Chinese Seafarers' Party Headquarters and Union had made great achievements in working for workers, especially under the leadership of Special Commissioner Yang, and there had been remarkable progress. He felt very comforted by Special Commissioner Yang and all comrades' efforts to seek welfare for workers. He was attending two conferences this time, the International Labor Conference and the Maritime Conference. There were many issues to be raised and discussed in these two conferences. The International Labor Conference is an organization shared by international laborers, so many international labor issues also need to be resolved at this conference. In general, the situation of Chinese labor issues is different from that of general international labor issues. The international labor issues were simply a matter of labor and capital, while Chinese labor issues involved both labor and capital issues and the issue of imperialist oppression and exploitation. Mr. Liu and Mr. Wang had clearly instructed them to demand the liberation of the Chinese nation, and they would naturally strive to do their best with sincerity. However, Xuefan knew that he had shallow knowledge and limited abilities, and he could not achieve great results by relying on personal strength alone. Therefore, he hoped that all comrades present would provide guidance at all times so that he could achieve considerable success at this conference and make a sincere report after returning home for the comrades' reference. He was honored to participate in this meeting today. In addition to expressing his gratitude, he respectfully toasted everyone.

Mr. Zhao's Reply

Zhao Banfu replied, stating that he was very grateful for the banquet hosted by the Seafarers' Party Headquarters, the Seafarers' Union, and various associations, and that he was unusually grateful for their kind hospitality. Over the years, there have been many conflicts between labor and capital, so the 21st conference was convened to resolve them. Banfu felt very uneasy about Special Commissioner Yang's (Hu) selection of him, feeling that his abilities and knowledge were lacking. Fortunately, Representative Zhu was successful in the Chinese labor community, and he was honored to follow Representative Zhu. The scope of rural bankruptcy has spread all over the world. Since Dr. Sun Yat-sen organized the scattered seafarers, the whole [group] has had a glorious performance in revolutionary history. Zhao had several important motions to propose at the International Maritime Conference, including the working hours of seafarers on ships, the protection of seafarers' diseases, and the payment of wages for seafarers' holidays. In addition, there were two other issues: (1) The inequality of wages between Chinese seafarers and foreign seafarers, and the fact that the treatment of seafarers with the same position on the same ship was always higher for foreign seafarers and lower for Chinese seafarers, which was very unfair in principle and would be raised at the Maritime Conference. (2) The contracting system should be abolished to reduce the exploitation of workers. He hoped that at this meeting, the suffering of Chinese seamen would be expressed and a fair judgment would be obtained. In addition, before and after the meeting, he planned to observe the situation of various seafarers for reference. However, Banfu felt that his talent and knowledge were limited, and he was afraid that he would not be able to bear this heavy responsibility. Fortunately, there was the Seafarers' Party Headquarters and the Seafarers' Union, which had a glorious history, all under the leadership of Special Commissioner Yang, and with the support of Representative Zhu, the result would certainly not be too bad. He borrowed the host's wine to express his gratitude. Then, Chen Haifeng gave a speech, the details of which were omitted.

Various Banks and Money Shops Receive Marked Notes: China and Communications Banks Continue as Before, Cancellation of Return to Be in Effect Until Contract Expiration; Other Banks Resolve Through Separate Consultations 95

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that Shanghai banks and money shops signed contracts with various note-issuing banks to receive marked notes. The method was 60% cash, 40% guarantee, or 100% cash, with the issuing bank rebating 40% interest. Since the implementation of the new currency system policy on November 4 of last year, various issuing banks, such as the China Industrial, China General Chamber of Commerce, and the four banks (Dalu, Yanzhou, Zhongnan, Jincheng), as well as the Kenye, Nongshang, and Siming banks, cancelled the marked note arrangement, leading to disputes. Now, these have been resolved through consultations. As for the China and Communications Banks, they are currently operating as before, but the procedure for cancelling the return of notes will be in effect until the expiration of the contract. The Banknote Association previously received an inquiry from the Tianjin Money Shops Association and has now replied, "Dear Sirs, We have received your letter inquiring about the resolution of our colleagues' receipt of marked notes from the China and Communications Banks. Please investigate and reply. We have investigated that the receipt of marked notes from the China and Communications Banks by our members is currently operating as before. The China and Communications Banks have not made any changes. We hereby reply accordingly, and we hope for your kind understanding."

Ye Gongchuo Requests Ban on Wanton Cooking and Eating of Cats and Dogs, Sends Special Letter to Fuding County Government to Prohibit 96

Reports indicate that dog restaurants and _ restaurants have been established in this city one after another. The affluence of these creatures' lives is beyond the reach of ordinary people. Yesterday, the China Animal Protection Association on Yunnan Road received a report from a charitable organization in Fuding County, Fujian Province, requesting a ban on the cooking and eating of cats and dogs in the county, in order to preserve life. The two situations present a striking contrast, one of affluence, the other of satisfying appetites. After receiving the report, the association's chairman, Ye Gongchuo, sent a letter to the county government to investigate and prohibit the practice. The original letter is as follows:

Dear Sirs, We have received reports that some residents in your county have been capturing, killing, cooking, and eating cats and dogs at will, harming beneficial animals. The situation is extremely dire. Please find a way to stop it. Cats and dogs are beneficial to humans and are not meant for consumption. For the sake of satisfying their appetites, people are wantonly killing creatures. This cruel custom is rampant and has a significant impact on people's hearts. Therefore, we are writing to request that the County Government promptly investigate and prohibit this practice, in order to benefit living beings and rectify people's hearts. We hope that you will investigate and reply to this letter. Respectfully, To the Fuding County Government.

New Novice Monks of Longhua Temple Beg for Alms Yesterday, Collected Enough Grain; Visited Lay Buddhist Forest and Buddhist Association; Bidding for Buddhist Cemetery Held Yesterday 97

Since Longhua Temple held the Great Ordination of a Thousand Buddhas, the number of new novice monks in this session has reached over 250. As a result, the number of mouths to feed is large, and there is a shortage of vegetarian food. Yesterday, they specially went to Buddhist Lay Forest, the Chinese Buddhist Association and other groups to beg for alms of vegetarian food. The details are as follows:

Novice Monks Beg for Alms

Yesterday at noon, the 250 novice monks of the temple, led by Abbot Xingkong, Supervisor Yongchan, and Deputy Abbot Hongkui, set out on foot from Longhua Temple. At around 2:00 PM, they arrived at the Buddhist Lay Forest on Xinmin Road. They placed the large porcelain bowls they were carrying in the corridor of the forest and began the Buddhist ritual of begging for alms. Li Jingwei, the head of general affairs of the forest, led forest friends Yuan Xilian, Xie Meizhi, and Pan Zongyuan in donating money and goods, which were placed in the bowls. The total amount reached over 200 yuan. At around 3:00 PM, after the ceremony, the novice monks went to the Chinese Buddhist Association on Hede Road and begged for alms in the same way. They returned to the temple as a group in the evening.

Cemetery Bidding

In addition, the Buddhist cemetery initiated by philanthropists Wang Yiting, Qu Wenliu, and Guan Jiong, among others, purchased 100 mu of land on Zhenda Road as a base. Construction work such as digging canals and filling land has been underway in recent days. Since advertisements were placed to solicit bids for the construction of tomb houses, bridges, gatehouses, funeral homes, and other projects, the bidding was held yesterday afternoon at the Buddhist Bookstore on Hede Road. As a result, the Zhang Changji Construction Company won the bid for construction and will start work immediately.

Business Houses in Tangjiawan Petition for Investigation of Violent Police Officers, Request Prompt Release of Innocents 98

Xin Xin News Agency reports that over a hundred stores, including Changda and Yongxingxiang on Zhaozhou Road in Tangjiawan, jointly petitioned the municipal government yesterday, requesting strict punishment of illegal police officers. The original text reads: (omitted above) It has been investigated that Mei Shunxing sesame oil store at No. 375 Zhaozhou Road brought in five bags of sesame seeds on the morning of April 17 this year. While temporarily placing them in front of the store, while the weighing process was ongoing, police officer No. 3833 suddenly stepped forward to interfere, stopping the weighing process, and instructed the store to immediately move the bags inside. The store owner, Liu Peiyuan, politely requested the police officer to allow him to finish weighing the bags and then he would move them inside, and requested leniency. Unexpectedly, the police officer slapped the store owner and kicked him. The store owner fled into the store, and the police officer chased after him, punching and kicking him indiscriminately. Onlookers gathered, many feeling indignant. The police officer, realizing his wrongdoing, tore his uniform with his hands and detained the store owner, Hu Peiyuan, in the West Gate Branch Bureau. The bureau's officer Huang, without investigating the matter in detail, sentenced him to fifteen days of detention, a fine of five yuan, and compensation for the uniform. We stores witnessed the incident and are extremely frightened. It is a fact that the police officer tore his uniform after committing the violence, as witnessed by us. Moreover, the store owner Wu Peiyuan is an honest and legitimate businessman, how could he dare to beat a police officer and willingly accept legal punishment? It is clear that he has been falsely accused and wronged. Such a grievance remains unaddressed, and police officers act tyrannically and disregard the law. If a thorough investigation is not conducted and strict punishment is not imposed, we merchants will all be in danger. Therefore, we jointly submit this petition, respectfully requesting that the authorities conduct a thorough investigation and promptly release the innocent, and severely punish the illegal police officer, in order to maintain local security and uphold the rule of law, which is in the public interest.

Binshan Native Association Petitions for Extension of Songhu Branch Line to Reach Baoshan City Directly from Paotaiwan, Hoping Construction Will Begin Soon to Achieve Multiple Benefits at Once 99

Da Gong News Agency reports that the Baoshan Native Association in Shanghai submitted a petition to the Nanjing Ministry of Railways yesterday, requesting the extension of the Songhu Railway branch line to directly reach Baoshan City in order to facilitate transportation. The petition reads: "Petition to respectfully request permission to extend the Songhu branch line of the Jinghu Railway to reach Doushan County Town, in order to benefit transportation and achieve prosperity. It is noted that

Our County of Baoshan

is located on the coast, guarding the mouth of the river, and is rich in strategic advantages. It is also adjacent to Shanghai, a commercial port, and enjoys the benefits of smooth flow. However, due to its remote location and obstructed transportation, the people's intelligence is closed off, like a remote place. To achieve prosperity, there is no way to realize it. Those with knowledge have long regarded it as a pity. The Association regards Baoshan as its homeland and feels the pain even more deeply. After repeated discussions among the members, it was unanimously agreed that prosperity should be the ultimate goal for Baoshan, and that developing transportation should be the primary task. Moreover, the benefits of Baoshan's revitalization are not only for the people of Baoshan to enjoy exclusively. The scope of dissemination

Can Be Considered Remarkable

The Association takes the liberty of presenting its views and saying a word to Your Ministry. It is noted that the current transportation lifeline of Baoshan relies solely on the Songhu branch line of the Jinghu Railway. The Songhu Line starts from Shanghai and ends at Paotaiwan in Wusong Town. Paotaiwan is still four Chinese miles away from Baoshan County Town. Usually, one must rely on rickshaws or walking to get there. However, travelers going up and down the road of this short distance often feel overwhelmed by fatigue. If bandits are rampant, people are even more hesitant to travel at night. If the Songhu branch line is extended to reach the bridgehead outside the South Gate of Baoshan County Town, then

Smooth and Convenient Transportation

can be expected, and revitalization can be awaited. Paotaiwan to the South Gate of Baoshan is less than two kilometers away. The route is flat, and it is easy to repair the roadbed and lay the tracks. The estimated cost of the line, calculated at ten mu of land in a straight line, is only 2,000 yuan, assuming a price of 200 yuan per mu. In addition, the cost of road construction, based on ordinary standards, is calculated at 10,000 yuan per Chinese mile. Now the road line is only one kilometer and one-third long, and the cost is no more than 33,300 yuan. The cost of building station houses and increasing staff is at most 12,000 yuan. In summary,

Various Expenses

A sum of 50,000 yuan is enough. Although this is not entirely credible and needs to be verified by experts, it seems that there should be no significant difference based on the actual situation. If it can be successfully completed, then Baoshan County Town can directly reach Shanghai, and the speed of transportation with the new Shanghai County will be like what? The low land price in Baoshan will inevitably induce entrepreneurs to eagerly invest heavily in building farms and factories. In the blink of an eye, the Greater Shanghai Plan will be completed, and Baoshan, close to the new port, will further change its old appearance and become more active. Its beauty is like. Furthermore, the scenery within the boundaries of Baoshan City,

The Scenery of the Yangtze River

is also worth mentioning. With convenient transportation, it will definitely attract people from afar to reside there, and there is a trend towards becoming a beautiful residential area. These two points alone are of no small benefit to Baoshan. If we talk about road maintenance, there will be more than enough surplus. Furthermore, Baoshan's southwest borders the Tai and Jia counties, where a motor vehicle avenue has been built. It cannot be smoothly connected to Songhu in the east. Since the Songhu area has always been known as the front line of national defense, if the road line can be extended, it can become a unified line in all directions, which is also beneficial to national defense. Multiple Benefits at Once

is not an exaggeration. The Association is aware of this and does not dare to remain silent. This small expenditure should not affect the overall situation. Moreover, this initiative is of great benefit to the local and national governments, and there should be no delay. Therefore, we respectfully request that Your Ministry instruct the Jinghu Railway Bureau to dispatch personnel to survey the route and start construction as soon as possible, in order to achieve success. On the 13th of this month, a husband and wife checked into the Nanyang Hotel at No. 394 North Zhejiang Road, and designated Room 22 as their lodging. Yesterday at around 10:00 AM, the wife suddenly went out, leaving only Wang in the room for lunch. Until evening, Peng had not returned to the hotel, and Wang Caiying in the room was also completely silent, and did not call the waiter to prepare dinner. Therefore, the waiters were suspicious. Until about 9:00 PM that night, the waiters could not bear it anymore and went to knock on the door. However, there was no response for a long time. They immediately tried to open the door and enter, and found Wang lying stiffly in bed, already unconscious. An empty box of poison was left on the pillow. They knew it was a suicide, and immediately reported to the police station and sent Wang to the hospital. However, Wang died soon after due to severe poisoning. The body has been sent to the morgue for examination. Taxpayers' Association Sends Letter to French Municipal Council Requesting Cancellation of Harsh Taxes on Fen Wine Business; Tax Collectors Should Report Facts Accurately; Earnest Protection of Small Businesses is Requested 105

Shen Shi News reports that members of the Fen Wine Industry Association in the French Concession have successively claimed to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the French Concession that the French Municipal Council has recently been levying counter taxes on members of the industry and extorting a monthly tax of two yuan and eight jiao from small single-room liquor stores, which is an unbearable burden for merchants with limited business scopes. They requested that the association forward a letter to the French Municipal Council to cancel the aforementioned harsh taxes in order to maintain their businesses. After receiving the report, the association immediately sent a letter to the French Municipal Council requesting its cancellation. The reasons stated are as follows:

Counter Tax

The Fen Wine industry has never sold hot liquor, so there is no so-called counter tax. Occasionally, a small number of businesses set up one or two small counters to attract customers in order to maintain their storefronts. However, in reality, having a counter is equivalent to not having one, and it has no impact on business. Now that the French Municipal Council wants to levy a counter tax, it should immediately notify all relevant businesses that, in the future, all small counters that are merely for show should no longer be placed inside the store. If counters are absolutely necessary for maintaining the storefront, they should all pay the counter tax monthly according to the regulations of the Municipal Council. However, the Municipal Council's tax collectors should also verify the facts accurately and not report excessively (for example, Xiechang Tea and Liquor Store at No. 252, Xujiahui Road, has two and a half counters, but the tax collector reported five and a half). This is the first matter that should be earnestly protected.

Monthly Tax

The criteria for the monthly tax on the liquor industry, which is divided into different grades, is not stated anywhere. Under normal circumstances, small single-room liquor stores generally pay one yuan and four jiao per month. However, Zhen Xiangyong at No. 290, Beile Road, Zhen Xingyong at No. 450, Zhang Hongsheng at No. 180, Malang Road, Yu Taixiang at No. 14, Annajin Road, and Qing Xiangyu and other Fen liquor stores at No. 119, Ximen Road, all had their taxes increased from one yuan and four jiao to two yuan and eight jiao last year, and there were even cases of overcharging by several jiao. The French Municipal Council should promptly balance the monthly tax rates of the aforementioned liquor stores and clearly indicate the grading standards in detail to ensure fairness. This is the second matter that should be earnestly protected. The above two matters have been repeatedly reported by the Fen Wine Industry Association. It is requested that your Municipal Council consider the situation and resolve them promptly and provide a reply for notification.

Shanghai Silk Industry Bank Holds Shareholders Meeting Yesterday 108

Xin Sheng News reports that Shanghai Silk Industry Bank at No. 460, Hankou Road, has been established for six years. Yesterday afternoon at 2 p.m., the bank held its fifth annual general meeting of shareholders on the fourth floor of the Silk Industry Building. All directors, supervisors, deputy managers, and shareholders including Du Yuesheng, Chen Aishi, Xu Jilong, Pei Yunqing, Wang Boyuan, Wu Kaixian, Shen Qinzhai, Wu Yunxu, Wang Boying, Chen Ziming, Shou Yicheng, Feng Zhongqing, Ma Jiliang, and more than a hundred others attended. Chairman Wang Yansong led the ceremony and read the fifth annual business report, making a brief report, stating that: Fellow shareholders, in addition to what has been outlined in the printed business report regarding the bank's affairs over the past year, there are two points that need to be added to the report. First, banks originally aim to regulate surpluses and deficits, and facilitate circulation. In February of last year, the Silk Industry Association and other organizations in this city, recognizing the decline of commerce and industry and the exhaustion of finance, and the fact that business practices often rely on extending credit, which freezes capital and stagnates trade, jointly advocated for commercial acceptance drafts to alleviate financial difficulties. The goal was to shorten credit periods and increase currency circulation. The bank believes that the promotion of such drafts is closely related to the banking industry, as it can invisibly increase the circulation of currency and benefit all parties. Fearing that the significance of these drafts may not be understood by the general public, hindering their implementation, the bank, based on its desire to serve society, not only publicized their significance in newspapers and published sample commercial acceptance drafts for public research, but also recognized that if the banking industry does not set an example, it would lose the opportunity for conversion. In March, after an important meeting, the bank decided to accept the discounting of these drafts, established discounting procedures, and set up a discounting market. These commercial acceptance drafts meet the needs of commerce and industry. In the future, if all industries jointly promote them, cooperation from the financial industry will be needed to achieve full success. The bank decided to request the Banking Association to discuss and finalize a universal discounting plan when convening meetings, and to consult with the Silk Industry Association and other organizations at any time to promote the benefits. As a result of the bank's continuous advocacy, not only have various industries gradually adopted them, but the Banking Association, in response to the need, has also established a Bills Acceptance Office under the Joint Preparation Committee to promote discounting business. The bank has also joined the office as a member bank. In short, although the bank does not dare to claim to be the first to promote commercial acceptance drafts and bill discounting, it has fulfilled its responsibility to serve. Second, Item 5 of the resolution of the previous annual general meeting stated that, in order to strengthen the bank's strength and consolidate its foundation due to the increasing expansion of its business, it was proposed to increase capital by 800,000 yuan, combining with the original capital to form 2 million yuan. The case was unanimously passed. After the board of directors accepted the resolution, it contacted various parties. As of now, nearly 400,000 yuan has been discussed. Then Supervisor Xu Jilong reported on the accounts, and the supervisors were discussed and elected. Ge Shuqian and Chen Ziming were elected as scrutineers, and Shen Ji'en and Chen Qingzhao were elected as tellers. As a result of the election, Xu Jilong, Chen Aishi, Ge Shuqian, and Cheng Yongliu were elected as supervisors. The majority decided that Lu Zhengbing and Lu Bohong should be the two supervisors. Finally, tea and refreshments were served, and photos were taken before the meeting adjourned.

Xiang Sheng Automobile Hijacked, Unknown for What Purpose; Reports Filed to Police for Investigation and Apprehension 115

At 10:37 p.m. last night, the 12th branch of Xiang Sheng Automobile Company at No. 277, Fuxu Road, French Concession, was suddenly visited by an uninvited customer, about 20 years old, wearing a blue cloth shirt and trousers and a melon-shaped hat, claiming to need to rent a car to go to the west of Shanghai. The company's accountant ordered driver Wang Xinbao (local) to drive a No. 4963 car, registered as No. 18406 in the concession (No. 4806 in the Chinese area). After the driver obtained the signed slip from the accountant, the uninvited customer immediately sat in the car and ordered it to drive west. After passing Beidichen Road to the gate of the Orphanage Grand Theater, the uninvited customer instructed to stop the car. A well-dressed man, around 30 years old, was waiting there on the sidewalk. Upon seeing the car stop, he also calmly boarded the car and ordered it to drive to Hongqiao. The driver obeyed and drove. When the car arrived near Kaixuan Road, Hongqiao Road, the two men ordered to stop the car. As soon as the driver turned to look back, the two men suddenly revealed their hideous faces, forcing the driver to get out of the car. Driver Wang Xinbao, seeing this situation, realized he had encountered bandits. Seeing the area was unusually desolate, he had no way to resist and sullenly got out of the car. The uninvited customer in short clothes drove away and disappeared in an instant. Helpless, the driver rushed to the nearby Fahua Township Public Security Bureau to report the incident. The branch office notified Xiang Sheng's head office, which reported to the French patrol room, requesting pursuit and apprehension. The French patrol room then notified the public concession's patrol rooms and the municipal public security bureau's branch offices and police stations, requesting them to pay attention to intercepting the car. As of the time of this newspaper's publication, the car was still missing.
